    kvu      kv    w i   
             
 abhidhammapiṭake 
 kathāvatthuppakaraṇaṃ 
  
 paṭhamo bhāgo 
  
 abhidhammapiṭake 
  
 kathāvatthuppakaraṇa 
  
 namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammā sambuddhassa  
  
 paṭhamo vaggo 
  
       
  
 puggalakathā 
  
    sakavādipucchā  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti     
  
 paravādipaṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sakavādianuyogo  yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho   tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti     
  
 paravādipaṭikkhepo  nahevaṃ vattabbe  
  
 sakavādiniggaho  ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
  
  
  
    sacchikaṭṭhaparamaṭṭhenāti  syā 
    sacchikaṭṭho paramaṭṭho  syā 
  
           
  
 anulomaṭhapanā  hañcī puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 anulomapāpanā  tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho   tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthoti  
 anuloma āropanā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
 paṭilomaṭhapanā  no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 paṭilomapāpana  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭiloma āropanā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
 anuloma pañcakaṃ  
  
    paravādipucchā  puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti   
  
 sakavādipaṭiññā  āmantā             
 paravādianuyogo  yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭikkhepo  nahevaṃ vattabbe  
 paravādipaṭikammaṃ  ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ  
  
  
  
    saccikaṭṭho paramaṭṭho  syā 
    sacchikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  syā  
  
           
  
 anulomaṭhapanā  hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 anulomapāpanā  tena vata re vattabbe so saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 anuloma āropanā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 paṭilomaṭhapanā  no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭiloma āropanā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
 paṭikammacatukkaṃ 
  
    pa  ni  tvaṃ ce pana maññasi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  tena tava tattha hetāya paṭiññāya hevaṃ paṭijānantaṃ hevaṃ niggahetabbe atha taṃ niggaṇhāmi  suniggahīto ca hosi  
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggelo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭha paramatthena  
  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalonūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
           
  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā             
  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti idaṃ te micchā  
  
 niggaha catukkaṃ  
  
    pa  u  ese ce dunniggahite hevamevaṃ tattha dakkhā  vattabbe kho puggaloupalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  no ca mayaṃ tayā tattha hetāya paṭiññāya hevaṃ paṭijānattā hevaṃ niggahetabbaṃ  atha maṃ niggaṇhāsi  dunniggahitā ca homa  
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
             
  
 yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
 pari  ṭha  no ca pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti idaṃ te micchā  
  
 upanayanacakukkaṃ             
  
    pa  niga  na hevaṃ niggahatabbe  tena hi yaṃ niggaṇhāsi  
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 anu  pā tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho  tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati   saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalouppalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
  
    nūpalabbhati p  t  s   
  
             
  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccakaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo uppalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti idaṃ te micchā  
  
 nigamanaṃ  tena hi ye kate niggahe se niggahe dukkaṭe sukate paṭikimme  sukata paṭipādanāti 
  
 nigamana   catukkaṃ  
  
 paṭhamo niggaho  
  
 pa  pu  puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 pa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
 anu  ṭha hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalā nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo            saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā 
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
  
  
    niggamana  sīmu  machasaṃ  
  
             
  
 no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalababhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  micchā  
  
 paccanika pañcakaṃ  
  
    sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā āmantā  
 sa  anu  yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe 
 sa  paṭikamma  ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ  
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micachā  paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe pugagalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 paṭikammacatukkaṃ             
             
  
    sa  ni  tvā ce pana maññasi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramatto tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  tena tava tattha hetāya paṭiññāya hevaṃ paṭijānantaṃ hevaṃ niggahetabbe  atha taṃ niggaṇhāmi  suniggahito ca hosi  
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
   anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggaloupalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti idaṃ te micchā  
  
 niggaha catukkaṃ  
  
    sa  u  ese ce dunniggahite hevamevaṃ tattha dakkha  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tatoso puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  no ca mayaṃ tayā tattha hetāya paṭiññāya hevaṃ paṭijānantā hevaṃ niggahetabbā  atha maṃ niggaṇhāsi  dunniggahitā ca homa  
  
             
  
 anu  ṭha  hañca puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭha paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati            saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramatto tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikatthaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti idaṃ te micchā  
  
 upanayana catukkaṃ 
  
     sa  ni  na hevaṃ niggahetabbe  tena hi yaṃ niggaṇhāsi  
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 anu  pā  tena vata re cattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati scacikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
             
  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti 
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalaba bhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe yo saccikaṭṭho paramattho tato so puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti idaṃ te micchā  
 nigamanaṃ  tena hi ye kate niggahe se niggahe dukkaṭe  sukate paṭikamme  sukatā paṭipādanāti  
  
 nigamana catukkaṃ 
  
 dutiyo niggaho             
  
     sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa anu  sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa  avajānanā  na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 sa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ 
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
             
  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe sabbattha puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā pe 
  
 tatiyo niggaho  
  
     sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sabbadā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa  pavi  na havaṃ vattabbe  
 sa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ 
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe sabbadā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparatthena  no ca vattabba sabbadā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe sabbadā puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe sabbadā            puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā pe 
  
 catuttho niggaho  
  
             
  
 sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  sabbesu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 sa  ni  ājanāhi niggahaṃ  
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe sabbesu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe sabbosu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe sabbosu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbepuggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena no ca vattabbe sabbesu puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  pe 
  
 pañcamo niggaho  
  
     pa  pu  puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu sabbattha puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 pa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
             
  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe sabbattha puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe sabbatta puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā              
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe sabbattha puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe sabbattha puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
 chaṭṭho niggaho 
  
     pa  pu  puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  sabbadā puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 pa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ 
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe sabbadā puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe sabbadā puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
  
             
  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe sabbadā puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe sabbadā puggalo nūpalababati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  pe 
  
 sattamo niggaho 
  
     pa  pu  puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  sabbesu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe              
 pa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ 
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe sabbesu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe sabbesu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe sabbesu puggalonūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe sabbesu puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti micchā pe 
  
 aṭṭhamo niggaho 
  
             
  
     sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti 
 pa  paṭi  hevaṃ vattabbe 
 sa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ 
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbeaññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccakaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe aññaraṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena              no ca vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti micchā pe 
  
        sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe saññā ca upalabbhati pesaṅkārā ca upalabbhanti peviññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
             
  
 sa  anu  aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe 
 sa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe  aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  aññño puggaloti  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  añño puggaloti  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viñññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā pe 
  
     sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  cakkhāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe sotāyatanañca upalanabbhati  pe ghānāyatanañca upalabbhati pe jivhāyatanañca upalabbhati pekāyāyatanañca upalabbhati pe rūpāyatanañca upalabbhati pesaddāyatanañca upalabbati pe gandhāyatanañca upalabbhati perasāyatanañca upalabbhati pe phoṭṭhabbāyatanañca upalabbhati pemanāyatanañca upalabbhati pe dhammāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe 
  
             
  
        sa  pu  cakkhudhātu ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pesotadhātu ca upalabbhati pe ghānadhātu ca upalabbhati pejivhādhātu ca upalabbhati pekāyadhātu ca upalabbhati perūpadhātu ca upalabbhati pe sadda dhātu ca upalabbhati pegandhadhātu ca upalabbhati pe rasadhātu ca upalabbhati pephoṭṭhabbadhātu ca upalabbhati pe 
  
 sa  pu  cakkhuviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati pe sotaviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati peghānaviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati pejivhāviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati pekāyaviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati pe manodhātu ca upalabbhati pe dhammadhātu ca upalabbhati pemanoviññāṇadhātu ca   upalabbhati pemanoviññāṇadhātu  ca upalabbhati    pesaccikaṭṭhaparamatthena             
 pe 
  
     cakkhundriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pesotindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena peghanindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe kāyindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe manindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pejīvitindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe itthindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe purisindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe sukhindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe dukkhindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pesomanassindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe 
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa  anu  aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe  
  
 sa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
  
  
    manoviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati dhammadhātu ca upalabbhati sacchikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe machasaṃ  sīmu  syā  
  
             
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
 aññāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 sa  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  aññopuggaloti micchā  
  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 paṭi  pā  no ca pana vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā ti  
  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā  pe 
  
     pa  pu  puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 pa  pu  vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā ti  
  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 pa  anu  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe 
  
 pa  paṭikammaṃ  ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ  
  
             
  
 pa  ṭha  hañci vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  rūpañcupalababhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā              
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 pa  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 pa  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā pe 
  
     pa  pu  puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 pa  pu  vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  vedanā ca upalabbhati pe saññā ca upalabbhati pe saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti pe viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 pa  anu  añññāṃ viññāṇaṃ  aññe puggaloti  
  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe  
  
 pa  paṭikammaṃ  ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ  
  
             
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  viññānagñca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā  
  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 pa  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthipuggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 pa  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vatactabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ  viññāṇaṃ añño puggaloti micchā pe 
  
          pa  pu  puggalo nūupalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 pa  pu  vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  cakkhāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe sotāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  dhammāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe 
  
 cakakhudhātu ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe kāyādhātu ca upalabbhati pe rūpadhātu ca upalabbhati pe phoṭṭhabbadhātu ca upalabbhati pe cakkhuviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati pe manodhātu ca upalabbhati pe dhammadhātu ca upalabbhati pemanoviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati    saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe 
  
    manoviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati dhammadhātu ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  machasaṃ  sīmu  syā pe 
  
              
  
 cakkhundriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe sotindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe aññindriyañca   upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe

 anu  ṭha  hañci vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitaṃya paṭipanno  aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā  
  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggaloti

 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā pe 
  
 suddhikasaṃsandanā  
  
    aññātāvindriyañca  sīmu  syā  
  
             
  
     sa  pu  rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññaṃ vedanāti  
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
  
 sa  pucchā  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa  anu  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe  
  
 sa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññā vedanā  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññā vedanā  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā              
  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññā vedanā  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpaṃca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
             
  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññā vedanā  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā pe 
  
         sa  pu  rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saññā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññaṃ viññāṇanti  
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa  anu  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabe  
  
 sa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā  
  
             
  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā ti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti micchā  pe 
  
     sa  pu  vedanā upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saññā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe saṅkhārā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe 
  
 saññā upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti peviññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe 
  
 saṅkhārā upalabbhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe saññā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe 
  
 sa  pu  viññāṇaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe saññāca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  añño saṅkhārāti  pe añño saṅkhārāti  pe 
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
             
  
 sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā ti

 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe              
 sa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
 anu  ṭha  hañci viññāṇaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  añño saṅkārā  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  palabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho viññāṇaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  aññe saṅkhārā  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā 
  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vanattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe viññāṇaṃ viññāṇaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  aññe saṅkhārā  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho viññāṇaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saṅkhārā ca upalabbhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  aññe saṅkhārā  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā pe 
  
             
  
      sa  pu  cakkhāyatanaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  sotāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pedhammāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pecakkhāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe manāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe 
  
 cakkhudhātu upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  sotadhātu ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe dhammadhātu ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe sotadhātu ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe 
  
 dhammadhātu upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  cakkhudhātu ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe manoviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe 
             
 sa  pu  cakkhundriyaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  sotindirayañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  peaññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pesotindriyaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe 
  
 aññātāvindriyaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  cakkhundriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe aññindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  aññaṃ aññindriyanti  
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa  anu  aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe  
  
 sa  ni  ājānāhi nighaṃ  
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci aññātāvindriyaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  aññaṃ aññindriyaṃ  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
             
  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggalo  ti  
  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho aññātāvindriyaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  aññaṃ aññindriyaṃ  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā 
  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe aññātāvindriyaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  aññaṃ aññindriyaṃ  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā ti  
  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho aññātāvindriyaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  aññaṃ aññindriyaṃ  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā  pe 
  
      pa  pu  rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññā vedanāti  
  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā              
 pa  pu  vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  rūpañcupalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthanāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
             
  
 pa  anu  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 pa  paṭikammaṃ  ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ 
 anu  ṭha  hañci rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññāvadanā  vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  
  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññā vedanā  vuttaṃ bhagavā  atthi puggalo atta hitāya paṭipanno  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti micchā  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti  
  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe rūpaṃ  upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññā vedanā  vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ rūpaṃ aññā vedanā  vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthipuggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti micchā  pe 
             
  
     pa  pu  rūpaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saññā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saṅkhārā ca upalabbhnati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe 
  
 vedanā upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saññā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saṅkhārā ca upalabbhnati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe 
  
 saññā upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saṅkhārā             ca upalababhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe 
  
 saṅkhārā upalabbhanti saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  viññāṇañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saññā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe 
  
 viññāṇaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  rūpañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  vedanā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saññāca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  saṅkhārā ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe 
  
 cakkhāyatanaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  sotāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pe dhammāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe bhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe 
  
 sotāyatanaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  dhammāyatanaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe cakkhāyatanañca upalabbhati pe manāyatanañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe  
  
 cakkhudhātu upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  sotadhātu ca upalabbhati pe dhammadhātu ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe 
  
 sotadhātu upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  dhammadhātu upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  pecakkhudhātu ca upalabbhati pemanoviññāṇadhātu ca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe 
  
             
  
 pa  pu cakkhundriyaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  sotindriyañca upalabbhati peaññātāvindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena pe 
  
 sotindriyaṃ upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññātāvindriyaṃ upalabbhati pecakkhundriyañca upalabbhati pe aññindriyañca upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthena  aññaṃ aññātāvindriyaṃ  aññaṃ aññindriyanti

 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipannoti

      pa  pu  puggalo nūpalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  pu  vuttaṃ bhagavatā atti puggalo attahitāya paṭipannoti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  rūpasmiṃ puggalo pe aññatra rūpā puggalo pepuggalasmiṃ             rūpaṃ pe vedanā puggalo pevedanāya puggalo pe aññatra vedanāya puggalo pepuggalasmiṃ vedanā pe saññā puggalo pe saññāya puggalo peaññatra saññāya puggalo pe puggalasmiṃ saññā pesaṅkhārā puggalo pesaṅkhāresu puggalo peaññatra saṅkhārehi puggalo pepuggalasmiṃ saṅkhārā peviññāṇaṃ puggalo pe viññāṇasmiṃ puggalo pe aññatra viññāṇā puggalo pe puggalasmiṃ viññāṇanti  
  
             
  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabeba  
 pa  paṭikammaṃ  ajānāhi paṭikammaṃ 
 anu  ṭha  hañci vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe puggalasmiṃ viññāṇanti  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  no ca vattabbe puggalasmiṃ viññānanti micchā  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe puggalasmiṃ viññāṇanti  
 paṭi pā  no ca vata re vattabbe vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipannoti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  no ca vattabbe puggalasmiṃ viññāṇanti micchā pe

 pa  pu  vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipannoti

 pa  anu  cakkhāyatanaṃ puggalo pe cakkhāyatanasmiṃ puggalo peaññatra cakkhāyatanā puggalo pe puggalasmiṃ cakkhāyatanaṃ pe dhammāyatanaṃ puggalo pedhammāyatanasmiṃ puggalo peaññatra dhammāyatanā puggalo pe puggalasmiṃ dhammāyatanaṃ pe 
  
 cakkhudhātu puggalo pe cakkhudhātuyā puggalo pe aññatra cakkhudhātuyā puggalo pe puggalasmiṃ cakkhudhātu pemanoviññāṇadhātu puggalo pemanoviññāṇadhātuyā puggalo pe aññatra manoviññāṇadhātuyā puggalo pepuggalasmiṃ manoviññāṇadhātu pe 
  
  
  
    upalabbhati  sīmu  
             
  
 cakkhundriyaṃ puggalo pe cakkhundriyasmiṃ puggalo peaññatra cakkhundriyā puggalo pe puggalasmiṃ cakkhundriyaṃ peaññātāvindriyaṃ puggalo pe aññātāvindriyasmiṃ puggalo pe aññatra aññātāvindriyasmiṃ puggalo peaññatra aññātāvindriyā puggalo pe puggalasmiṃ aññātāvindriyanti

 pa  paṭikammaṃ  ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ

 catukkanaya saṃsandanaṃ  
  
      sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  puggalo sappaccayo pe puggalo appaccayo pepuggalo saṅkhato pe puggalo asaṅkhato pepuggalo sassato pe puggalo asassato pe puggalo sanimitto pe puggalo animittoti  
  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe

 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 lakkhaṇayuttikathā  
  
      sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati  upalabbhati puggaloti  
 pa  paṭiññā  puggalo upalabbhati  upalabbhati kehici puggalo  kehici na puggaloti  
 sa  anu  puggalo kehici upalabbhati  kehici na upalabbhatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  puggalo saccikaṭṭho  saccikaṭṭho puggaloti  
 pa  paṭiññā  puggalo saccikaṭṭho  sacacikaṭṭho kehici puggalo  kehici na puggaloti              
 sa  anu  puggalo kehici saccikaṭṭho  kehici na saccikaṭṭhoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  puggalo vijjamāno  vijjamāno puggaloti  
 pa  paṭiññā  puggalo vijjamāno  vijjamāno kehici puggalo  kehici na puggaloti  
 sa  anu  puggalo kehici vijjamāno  kehici na vijjamānoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
             
  
      sa  pu  puggalo saṃvijjamāno  saṃvijjamāno puggaloti  
 pa  paṭiññā  puggalo saṃvijjamāno  saṃvijjamāno kehici puggalo  kehici na puggaloti  
 sa  anu  puggalo kehici saṃvijjamāno  kehici na saṃvijjamānoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  puggalo atthi  atthi puggaloti  
 pa  paṭiññā  puggalo atthi  atthi kehici puggalo  kehici na puggaloti  
 sa  anu  puggalo kehici atthi  kehici natthiti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  puggalo atthi  atthi na sabbo puggaloti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  puggalo natthi  natthi na sabbo puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 vacanasodhanaṃ

      sa  pu  kāyoti vā sarīranti vā  sarīranti vā kāyoti vā  kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāteti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  pu  puggaloti vā jīvoti vā  jīvoti vā puggaloti vā puggalaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se   ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjajateti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  pu  añño kāyo añño puggaloti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 sa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
  
  
    ucchinno     
    ese ese  pu  
             
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci kāyoti vā sarīranti vā  sarīranti vā kāyoti vā  kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte  puggaloti vā jīvoti vā  jīvoti puggaloti vā puggalaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese             se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte añño kāyo añño puggalo  
  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti  
  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho kāyoti vā sarīranti vā  sarīranti vā kāyoti vā kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte  puggaloti vā jīvoti vā  jīvoti vā puggaloti vā puggalaṃ appiyaṃ karitvāese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte  añño kāyo añño puggalo  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti micchā  
  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti  
  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe kāyoti vā sarīranti vā  sarīranti vā kāyoti vā kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte  puggaloti vā jīvoti vā  jīvoti vā  puggaloti vā puggalaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte  añño kāyo añño puggaloti  
  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho kāyotivā sarīranti vā  sarīranti vā kāyoti vā kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte  puggaloti vā jīvoti vā  jīvoti vā puggaloti vā puggalaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte  añño kāyo añño puggalo  no ca vattabbe aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti micchā pe 
  
               
  
 pa  pu  kāyoti vā sarīranti vā  sarīranti vā kāyoti vā kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāteti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  pu  vuttaṃ bhagavatā atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipannoti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  pu  añño kāyo añño puggaloti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe  
 pa  paṭikammaṃ  ājānāhi paṭikammaṃ  
 anu  ṭha  hañci kāyoti vā sarīranti vā  sarīranti vā kāyoti vā kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte  vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe añaño kāyo añño puggaloti  anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho kāyoti vā sarīranti vā  sarīranti vākāyoti vā kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte  vuttaṃ bhagavatā              atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  no ca vattabbe añño kāyo añño puggaloti micchā  
 paṭi  ṭha  no ce pana vattabbe añño kāyo añño puggaloti  
 paṭi  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe kāyoti vā sarīranti vā  sarīranti vā kāyoti vā kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte  vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipannoti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho kāyoti vā sarīranti vā  sarīranti vākāyoti vā kāyaṃ appiyaṃ karitdvā ese se ekaṭṭhe same samabhāge tajjāte  vuttaṃ bhagavatā  atthi puggalo attahitāya paṭipanno  no ca vattabbeañño kāyo añño puggaloti micchā pe 
  
 paññattānuyogo  
  
             
  
      sa  pu  puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokaṃ paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  so puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  pu  puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokaṃ paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokaṃ imaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  añño puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  puggalo savdhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  so ca añño ca sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  neva so sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti              
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  so puggalo sandhāvati  añño puggalo sandhāvati  so ca aññoca sandhāvati  neva so sandhāvati  na añño sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
             
  
      pa  pu  na vattabaṃbaṃ puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  pu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  
 sattakkhattu paramaṃ sandhāvitvāna puggalo dukkhassantakaro hoti sabbasaññojanakkhayā ti  attheva suttantoti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  ni  tena hi puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
  
      pa  pucchā  na vattabbaṃ puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  pucchā  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  anamataggoyaṃ bhikkhave saṃsāro  pubbā koṭina paññāyati avijjānīvaraṇānaṃ sattānaṃ taṇhāsaññojanānaṃ sandhāvataṃ saṃsaratanti   attheva suttantoti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  ni  tena hi puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
  
      sa  pu  puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  a  sveva puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭi  nahevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  sveva puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokāimaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  pu  atthi koci manusso hutvā devo hotīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sveva manusso so devoti              
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
             
  
      sa  pu  sveva manusso so devoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  ā  manusso hutvā devo hoti  devo hutvā manusso hoti  manussabhuto añño  devo añño  manussabhuto svāyaṃ svāyaṃ sandhāvatīti micchā pe 
 sa  ni  sace hi sandhāvati sveva puggalo ito cuto paraṃ lokaṃ anañño  hevaṃ   maraṇaṃ na hehīti  pāṇātipātopi nūpalabbhati  kammaṃ atthi  kammapivāko atthi  katānaṃ kammānaṃ vipāko atthi  kusalākusale vipaccamāne svevāyaṃ sandhāvatīti micchā  
  
      sa  pu  sveva puggalo savdhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi koci manusso hutvā yakkho hoti pepeto hoti pe nerayiko hoti petiracchānagato hoti peoṭṭho hoti pegoṇo hoti pegadrabho hoti pesūkaro hoti pe mahiso   hotīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sveva manusso so mahisoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  anu  sveva manusso so mahisoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 saka  ā  manusso hutvā mahiso   hoti  mahiso hutvā manusso hoti  manussabhuto añño  mahiso añño  manussabhuto svevāyaṃ sandhāvatīti micchā pe 
 sa  niga  sace hi sandhāvati sveva puggalo ito cuto paraṃ lokaṃ anañño  hevaṃ maraṇaṃ na hehīti  pāṇātipātopi nūpalabbhati  kammaṃ atthi  kammavipoko atthi  katānaṃ kammānaṃ vipāko atthi  kusalākusale vipaccamāne svevāyaṃ sandhāvatīti micchā  
  
  
  
    hetaṃ  aṭṭhakathā  
    mahiṃso  machasaṃ

 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
             
  
 sa  anu  hatthacchinno hatthacchinnoca hoti  pādacchinno pādacchinnoca hoti  hatthapādacchinno hatthapādacchinnoca hoti  kaṇṇacchinno pe nāsacchinno pekaṇṇanāsacachinno pe aṅgulicchinno pe aḷacchinno pe kaṇḍaracchinno pe kuṇihatthako pe kuṭṭhiyo pegaṇdhiyo pekilāsiyo pe sosiyo pe apamāriyo peoṭṭho pegoṇo pe gadrabho pe sūkaro pemahiso mahisova hotīti

 pa  pu  nanu sotāpanto puggalo manussalokā cuto devalokaṃ upapanno tatthapi sotāpannoca hotīti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  ṭha  hañci sotāpānno puggalo manussalokā vuto devalokaṃ upapanno tatthapi sotāpannoca hoti  
 pa  pā  tena vata re vattabbe sveva puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 sa  anu  sotāpanno puggalo manussalokā cuto devalokaṃ upapanno tatthapi sotāpannoca hotīti katvā tena ca kāraṇena sveva puggalovdhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokānti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  pu  sotāpanno puggalo manussalokā cuto devalokaṃ upapanno tatthapi manusso hotīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  sveva puggalo sandhāvati asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ parasmā lokā imaṃ lokanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
             
  
 sa  pu  anañño avigato sandhāvatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  pu  anañño avigato savadhāvatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  pu  hatthacchinno hatthacchinnova hoti  pādācchinno pādacchinnova hoti  hthapādacchinno hatthapādacchinnova hoti  kannacchinno pe nāsacchinno pekaṇṇanāsacchinno peaṅgulicchinno pe aḷacchinno pekaṇḍaracchinnopekuṇihatthako pe phaṇahatthako pekuṭṭhiyo pe gaṇḍiyo pekilāsiyo pe sosiyo pe apamāriyo pe oṭṭhā pegoṇo pegaidrako pe sūkaro pe mahiso mahisova hotīti  
  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe

 sa  pu  saviññāṇo savdhāvatīti

 sa  pu  taṃ jīvaṃ taṅ sarīranti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe

 khandhesu bhijjamānesu 
 so ce bhijjati puggalo 
 ucchedā bhavati diṭṭhi 
 yā buddhena vivajjitā  
  
 khandhesu bhijjamānesu 
 no ce bhijjati puggalo  
 puggalo sassato hoti  
 nibbānena samasamoti  
  
 gati anuyogo

 pa  anu  pañcavokārabhave pañceva puggalāti

      sa  pu  yathā rukkhaṃ upādāya chāyāya paññatti  evamevaṃ rūpaṃ upādāya puggalassa paññattīti  
 yathā rukkhaṃ upādāya chāyāya paññatti  rukkhopi anicco  chāyāpi aniccā  evamevaṃ rūpaṃ upādāya puggalassa paññatti  rūpampi aniccaṃ  puggalopi aniccoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  pu  yathā rukkhaṃ upādāya chāyāya paññatti  añño rukkho  aññā chāyā  evamevaṃ rūpaṃ upādāya puggalassa paññatti  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  yathā gāmaṃ upādāya gamikassa paññatti  evamevaṃ rūpaṃ upādāya puggalassa paññattīti  
 yathā gāmaṃ upādāya gamikassa paññatti  añño gāmo  añño gamiko  evamevaṃ rūpaṃ upādāya puggalassa paññatti  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  yathā raṭṭhaṃ upādāya rañño paññatti  evamevaṃ rūpaṃ upādāya puggalassa paññattīti  
 yathā raṭṭhaṃ upādāya rañño paññatti  aññaṃ raṭṭhaṃ  añño rājā  evamevaṃ rūpaṃ upādāya puggalassa paññatti  aññaṃ rūpaṃ añño puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  yathā na nigaḷo negaḷiko  yassa nigaḷo so negaḷiko  evamevaṃ na rūpaṃ rūpavā  yassa rūpaṃ so rūpavāti  
 yathā na nigaḷo negaḷiko  yassa nigaḷo so negaḷiko  añño nigaḷo  añño negaḷiko  evamevaṃ na rūpaṃ rūpavā  yassa rūpā so rūpavā  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  añño rūpavāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
               
  
      sa  pu  citte citte puggalassa paññattīti

 sa  anu  dutiye cite uppanne na vattabbaṃ kumārakoti vā kumārikāti vāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  vattabbaṃ  
 sa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ  anu  ṭha  hañci dutiye cite uppanne na vattabbaṃ soti vā aññoti vā  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe dutiye cite uppanne na vattabbaṃ kumārakotivā kumārikāti vāti  
 anu  a  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho dutiye citte uppanne na vattabbaṃ soti vā aññoti vā  dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ kumārakoti vā kumārikāti vāti micchā  
 paṭi  ṭha  hañci vā pana dutiye citte uppanne vatactabbaṃ kumārakoti vā kumārikāti vā  
 paṭi  pā  tena vata re vattabbe dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ soti vā aññeti vā  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vacattabbe kho dutiye citte uppannena vattabbaṃ soti vā aññoti vā  dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ kumārakoti vā kumārikāti micchā  
      sa  pu  dutiye cite uppanne na vattabbaṃ soti vā aññoti vāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
                 
  
 sa  anu  dutiye citte uppanne na vattabbaṃ itthiti vā purisoti vā gahaṭṭhotivā pabbajitoti vā devoti vā manussoti vāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  vattabbaṃ  
 sa  ni  ājānāhi niggahaṃ  
 anu  ṭha  hañci dutiye citte uppanne na vattabbasoti vā aññoti vā  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe dutiye citte uppanne na vattabbaṃ devoti vā manussoti vāti  
 anu  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho dutiye citte uppanne na vattabbaṃsoti vā aññoti vā  dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ devoti vā manussoti vāti micchā  
 paṭi  ṭha  hañci vā pana dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ devoti vā manussoti vā  
 paṭi  pā  tena vata re vattabbe dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ soti vā aññoti vāti  
 paṭi  ā  yaṃ tattha vadesi  vattabbe kho dutiye citte uppanne na vattabbaṃ soti vā aññoti vā  dutiye citte uppanne vattabbaṃ devoti vā manussoti vāti micchā pe 
  
      pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā              
 pa  pu  nanu yo passati  yaṃ passati  yena passati  so passati  taṃ passati  tena passatīti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci yo passati yaṃ passati  yena passati  so passati taṃ passati tena passati  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
                 
  
      pa  pu  na vattabaṃbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  pu  nanu yo suṇāti pe yo ghāyati pe yo sāyati pe yo phūsati pe yo vijānāti yaṃ vijānāti yena vijānāti  so vijānāti taṃ vijānātitena vijānātīti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci yo vijānāti yaṃ vijānāti yena vijānāti  so vijānāti taṃ vijānāti tena vijānāti  anu  pā  tena vata             re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
      sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati saccikṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  pu  nanu yo na passati  yaṃ na passati  yena na passati  so na passati  taṃ na passati  tena na passatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci yo na passati yaṃ na passati yena na passati  so na passati taṃ na passati tena passati  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
      sa  pu  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  pu  nanu yo na suṇāti pe yo na ghāyati pe yo na sāyati pe yo na phusati pe yo na vijānāti yaṃ na vijānāti yena vijānāti  so na vijānāti taṃ na vijānāti tena na vijānātīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
               
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci yo na vijānāti yaṃ na vijānāti yena na vijānāti  so na vijānāti taṃ na vijānāti tena na vijānāti  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
      pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ  puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  pu  nanu vuttā bhagavatā  passāmahaṃ bhikkhave dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena satte cavamāne visuddhena atikkantamānusakena satte cavamāne uppajjamāne   hīne paṇīte suvaṇṇe dubbaṇṇe sugate duggate yathākammūpage satte pajānāmīti attheva suttantoti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  niga  tena hi puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
      sa  pu  vuttaṃ bhagavatā  passāmahaṃ bhikkhave dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena satte cavamāne uppajjamāne hīne paṇite suvaṇṇe dubbaṇne sugate duggate yathākammupage satte pajānāmī ti katvā teneva kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  pu  bhagavā dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena rūpā passati puggalaṃ passatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  rūpaṃ passati  
 sa  anu  rūpaṃ puggalo  rūpaṃ cavati rūpaṃ uppajjati  rūpaṃ yathākammūpaganti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  bhagavā dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena rūpaṃ passati puggalaṃ passatacīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  puggalaṃ passati  
  
  
    upapajjamāne  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
 sa  anu  puggalo rūpaṃ  rūpāyatanaṃ  rūpadhātu  nīlaṃ  pītakaṃ  lohitakaṃ  odātaṃ  cakkhuviññeyyaṃ  cakkhusmiṃ paṭihaññati  cakkhussa āpāthaṃ āgacchatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  pu  bhagavā dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānussakena rūpaṃ passati  puggalaṃ passatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  ubho passati sa  anu  ubho rūpaṃ  rūpāyatanaṃ  rūpadhātu  ubho nīlā  ubho pītakā  ubho lohitakā  ubho odātā  ubho cakkhuviññeyayā              ubho cakkhusmiṃ paṭihaññanti  ubho cakkhussa āpāthaṃ āgacchanti  ubho cavanti  ubho uppajjanti  ubo yathākammūpagāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe

 sa  anu  aññaṃ āpāyikaṃ dukkhaṃ añño āpāyikassa dukkhassa paṭisaṃvedīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      pa  pu  nerayikaṃ dukkhaṃ upalabbhatīti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  nerayikassa dukkhassa paṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 pa  pu  nerayikaṃ dukkhaṃ upalabbhatīti nerayikassa dukkhassa paṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  pa  anu  tassa paṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 sa  paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
      sa  pu  tassa paṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  tassa tasseva natthi dukkhassa antakiriyā  natthi vaṭṭupacchedo  natthianupādā parinibbānanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  nerayikaṃ dukkhaṃ upalabbhatīti nerayikassa dukkhassa paṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
               
  
 sa  anu  puggalo upalabbhatīti puggalassa paṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  nerayikaṃ dukkhaṃ upalabbhatīti nerayikassa dukkhassa paṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
             
 sa  anu  nibbānaṃ upalabbhatīti nibbānassa paṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  nerayikaṃ dukkhaṃ upalabbhatīti nerayikassa dukkhassa paṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  mahāpaṭhavī upalabbhatīti pe mahāsamuddo upalabbhatīti pesinerupabbatarājā upalabbhatīti pe āpo upalabbhatīti pe tejo upalabbhatītipe vāyo upalabbhatīti petiṇakaṭṭhavanappatayo upalabbhantīti tiṇakaṭṭhavanappatīnaṃ paṭisaṃvedī upalabbhantīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  nerayikaṃ dukkhaṃ upalabbhatīti nerayikassa dukkhassa paṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  aññaṃ nerayikaṃ dukkhaṃ  añño nerayikassa dukkhassa paṭisaṃvedīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  kalyāṇapāpakāni kammāni upalabbhantīti kalyāṇapāpakānaṃ kammānaṃ kattā kāretā vipākapaṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  so karoti so paṭisaṃvedetīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  pu  so karoti so paṭisaṃvedetīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sayaṃ kataṃ sukhadukkhanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
               
  
      sa  pu  kalyāṇapāpakāni kammāni upalabbhantiti kalyāṇapāpakānaṃ kammānaṃ kattā kāretā vipākapaṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  añño karoti  añño paṭisaṃvedetīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  pu  añño karoti  añño paṭisaṃvedetīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  paraṃ kataṃ sukhadukkhanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  kalyāṇapāpakāni kammāni upalabbhantiti kalyāṇapāpakānaṃ kammānaṃ kattā kāretā vipākapaṭisaṃvedī upalbhatīti  
             
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  so ca añño ca karonti  so ca añño ca paṭisaṃvedentīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  pu  so ca añño ca karonti  so ca añño ca paṭisaṃvedentīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sayaṃ katañca paraṃ katañca sukhadukkhanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  kalyāṇapāpakāni kammāni upalabbhantīti kalyāṇapāpakānaṃ kammānaṃ kattā kāretā vipākapaṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  neva so karoti na so paṭisaṃvedeti  na añño karoti na añño paṭisaṃvedetīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  pu  neva so karoti na so paṭisaṃvedeti  na añño karoti na añño paṭisaṃvedetīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
               
  
 sa  anu  asayaṃkāraṃ apara kāraṃ adhiccasamuppannaṃ sukhaṃ dukkhanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  kalyāṇapāpakāni kammāni upalabbhantīti  kalyāṇapāpakānaṃ kammānaṃkattā kāretā vipākapaṭisaṃvedī upalabbhatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  so karoti so paṭisaṃvedeti  añño karoti añño paṭisaṃvedeti  so ca añño ca karonti so ca añño ca paṭisaṃvedenti  na añño karoti na añño paṭisaṃvedetīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  pu  so karoti so paṭisaṃvedeti  añño karoti añño paṭisaṃvedeti  so ca aññoca karonti so ca añño ca paṭisaṃvedenti  neva so karoti na so paṭisaṃvedeti  na añño karoti na añño paṭisaṃvedetīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sayaṃkataṃ sukhadukkhaṃ  paraṃkataṃ sukhadukkhaṃ  sayaṃkatañca paraṃkatañca sukhadukkhaṃ  asayaṃkāraṃ aparaṃkāraṃ adhiccasamuppannaṃ sukhadukkhanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
            
      pa  pu  kammaṃ atthiti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  kammakārako atthīti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  kammaṃ atthīti kammakārako atthiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  tassa kārako atthiti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
               
      sa  pu  tassa kārako atthīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  tassa tasseva natthi dukkhassa antakiriyā  natthi 
 vaṭṭūpacchedo  natthi anupadāparinibbānanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  kammaṃ atthiti kammakārako atthiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  puggalo atthiti puggalassa kārako atthiti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbepe 
  
      sa  pu kammaṃ atthiti kammakārako atthiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nibbānaṃ atthiti nibbānassa kārako atthiti 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbepe 
  
      sa  pu  kammaṃ atthiti kammakārako atthiti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  mahāpaṭhavī atthiti pemahāsamuddo atthiti pe 
 sinerupabbatarājā atthiti pe āpo atthiti pe 
 tejo atthiti pe vāyo atthiti pe 
 tiṇakaṭṭhavanappatayo atthiti tiṇakaṭṭhavanappatīnaṃ kārako 
 atthīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
      sa  pu  kammaṃ atthiti kammakārako atthiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  aññaṃ kammaṃ  añño kammakārakoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
      pa  pu  vipāko atthiti  sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  pa  anu  vipākapaṭisaṃvedī atthiti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
               
  
      sa  pu  vipāko atthiti vipākapaṭisaṃvedī atthiti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  tassa paṭisaṃvedī atthiti  
             
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  pu  tassa paṭisaṃvedī atthiti  sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  tassa tasseva natthi dukkhassa antakiriyā  natthi vaṭṭupacchedo  natthi anupādā parinibbānanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  vipāko atthiti vipākapaṭisaṃvedī atthiti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  puggalo atthiti puggalassa paṭisaṃvedī atthiti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  vipāko atthiti vipākapaṭisaṃvedī atthiti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  nibbānaṃ atthiti nibbāna paṭisaṃve atthiti  di 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  vipāko atthiti vipākapaṭisaṃvedī atthiti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  mahāpaṭhavī atthiti pemahāsamuddo atthiti pe 
 sineru pabbatarājā atthiti pe āpo atthiti pe 
 tejo atthiti pe vāyo atthiti pe 
 taṇakaṭṭhavanappatayo atthiti tiṇakaṭṭhavanappatīnaṃ paṭisaṃvedī 
 atthiti 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
      sa  pu  vipāko atthiti vipākapaṭisaṃvedī atthiti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  añño vipāko  añño vipākapaṭisaṃvedīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 kalyāṇavaggo paṭhamo  
  
               
  
      pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  pa  anu  nanu atthi koci iddhiṃ vikubbatīti     
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  anu  ṭha  hañci atthi koci iddhiṃ vikubbati  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā ti  
             
      pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  pa  anu  nanu atthi koci dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti pe 
 paracittaṃ jānāti   pe pubbenivāsaṃ anussarati pe 
 dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati pe āsavānaṃ khayaṃ 
 sacchikarotīti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  anu  ṭha  hañci atthi koci āsavānaṃ khayaṃ sacchikaroti  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti 
  
      sa  pu  atthi koci iddhiṃ vikubbatīti katvā tena ca kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  yo iddhiṃ vikubbati sveva pugga  yo iddhiṃ 
 na vikubbati na so puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  yo dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddhaṃ suṇati pe 
 yo paracittaṃ jānāti pe yo pubbenivāsaṃ 
 anussarati pe yo dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati pe yo āsavānaṃ khayaṃ sacchikaroti sveva puggalo  yo 
 āsavānaṃ khayaṃ na sacchikaroti na so puggaloti  
  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 abhiññānuyogo  
  
    iddhivikubbatīti      
    vijānāti  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
     pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  nanu mātā atthiti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  anu  ṭha  hañci mātā atthi  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhatīti  
  
      pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  pa  anu  nanu             
 pitā atthi pe bhātā atthi pe bhaginī atthi pe 
 khattiyo atthi pe brāhmaṇo atthi pevesso atthi pe suddo atthi pe gahaṭṭho atthi pepabbajito atthi pe devo atthi pe manusso atthiti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 anu  ṭha  hañci manusso atthi  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
      sa  pu  mātā atthiti katvā tena ca kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi koci na mātā hutvā mātā hotīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  pu  atthi koci na puggalo hutvā puggalo hotīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  atthi koci na pitā hutvā pe na bhātā hutvā 
 pe na bhaginī hutvā pe na khattiyo hutvā pe na 
 brāhmaṇo hutvā pe na vesso hutvā pe 
 na suddo hutvā pe na gahaṭṭho hutvā  pe 
 na pabbajito hutvā pe na devo hutvā pe 
 na manusso hutvā hutvā manusso hotīti  
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
               
  
 sa  anu  atthi koci na puggalo hutvā puggalo hotīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  mātā atthiti katvā tena ca kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati 
 saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā sa  pu  atthi koci mātā hutvā na mātā hotīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi koci puggalo hutvā na puggalo hotīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  atthī koci pitā hutvā pebhātā hutvā pebhaginī hutvā pekhattiyo hutvā pe brāhmaṇo hutvā pe vesso hutvā pesuddo hutvā pe gahaṭṭho hutvā pepabbajito hutvā pedevo hutvā pe manusesā hutvā na manusso hotī ti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthī koci puggalo hutvā na puggalo hotīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 ñātakānuyogo  
  
             
      pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  nanu sotāpanno atthiti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 paṭi  ṭha  hañci sotāpanno atthi  
 paṭi  pā  tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
      pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭha paramatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
               
  
 pa  anu  nanu sakadāgāmī atthi pe anāgāmī atthi pearahā atthipe ubhattābhṛgavimutto atthi pepaññāvimutto atthi pekāyasakkhi atthī pe diṭṭhippatto atthi pesaddhāvimutto atthi pe dhammānusārī atthi pesaddhānusārī atthīti  
  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 paṭi  ṭha  hañci saddhānusārī atthi  
 paṭi  pā  tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
      sa  pu  sotāpanno atthiti katvā tena ca kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi koci na sotāpanno hutvā sotāpanno hotīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi koci na puggalo hutvā puggalo hotīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  atthi koci na sakadāgāmī hutvā pe na anāgāmi hutvā pe na arahā hutvā pe na ubhatobhāga vimutto hutvā pe na paññāvimutto hutvā pe na kāyasakkhi hutvā pe na diṭṭhippatto hutvā pe na saddhāvimutto hutvā pe na dhammānusārī hutvā pe na saddhānusārī hutvā saddhānusārī hotīti  sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  atthi koci na puggalo hutvā puggalo hotīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
      sa  pu  sotāpānno atthi ti katvā tena ca kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
               
  
 sa  anu  atthi koci sotāpanno hutvā na sotāpanno hotī ti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  atthi koci puggalo hutvā na puggalo hotīti  
             
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  atthi koci sakadāgāmī hutvā peanāgāmi hutvā na na anāgāmī hotīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  atthi koṭi puggalo hutvā na puggalo hotiti 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 paṭivedhānuyogo 
  
      pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  nanu cattāro purisayugā aṭṭhapurisapuggalā atthiti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci cattāro purisayugā aṭṭhapurisapuggalā atthi  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattarebba puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenā ti  
  
      sa  pu  cattāro purisayugā aṭṭhapurisapuggalā atthiti katvā tena ca kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  cattāro purisayugā aṭṭhapurisapuggalā buddhapātubhāvā 
 pātubhavantīti  
 paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  puggalo buddhapātubhāvā pātubhavatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
               
  
     sa  pu  puggalo buddhapātubhāvā pātubhavatīti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  buddhassa bhagavato parinibbuto ucchinno puggalo  natthi 
 puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 saṅgahānuyogo  
  
      sa  pu  puggalo upilabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  puggalo saṅkhatoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  anu  puggalo asaṅkhatoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  anu  puggalo neva saṅkhato nāsaṅkhatoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  puggalo neva saṅkhato nāsaṅkhatoti  pa              
 paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  saṅkatañca asaṅkhatañca ṭhapetvā atthaññā tatiyā koṭīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  saṅkhatañca asaṅkhatañca ṭhapetvā atthaññā tatiyā koṭīti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā dvemā bhikkhave dhātuyo  katamā deva  saṅkhatā ca dhātu asaṅkhatā ca dhātu  imā kho bhikkhave dve dhātuyoti  attheva suttantoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  niga  tena hi na vattabaṃba saṅkhatañca asaṅkhatañca ṭhapetvā atthaññā tatiyā koṭī ti  
  
               
  
      sa  pu  puggalo neva saṅkhato nāsaṅkhatoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  aññaṃ saṅkhataṃ  aññaṃ asaṅkhataṃ  añño puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  khandhā saṅkhatā  nibbānaṃ asaṅkhataṃ  puggalo neva saṅkhato nāsaṅkhatoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  aññe bandhā  aññaṃ nibbānaṃ  añño puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  rūpaṃ saṅkataṃ  nibbānaṃ asaṅkhataṃ  puggalo neva saṅkhato 
 nāsaṅkhatoti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  aññaṃ rūpaṃ  aññaṃ nibbānaṃ  añño puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  vedanā pe saññā pe saṅkhārā pe viññāṇaṃ saṅkhataṃ  nibbānaṃ asaṅkhataṃ  puggalo neva saṅkhato nāsaṅkhatoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  aññaṃ viññāṇaṃ  aññaṃ nibbānaṃ  añño puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbepe 
  
      sa  pu  puggalassa uppādo paññāyati  vayo paññāyati  ṭhitassa aññathattaṃ paññāyatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  puggalo saṅkhatoti  
   p     
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
               
  
 sa  niga  vuttaṃ bhagavatā tiṇimāni bhikkhave saṅkhatassa saṅkhatalakkhanāni  saṅkhatānaṃ bhikkhave dhammānaṃ uppādo paññāyati  vayo paññāyati  ṭhitānaṃ   aññathattaṃ paññāyatīti  puggalassa uppādo paññāyāti  vayo paññāyati  ṭhitassa aññathattaṃ paññāyati  tena hi puggalo saṅkhatoti  
      sa  pu  puggalassa na uppādo paññāyati  na vayo paññāyati  na ṭhitassa aññathattaṃ paññāyatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  puggalo asaṅkhatoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  niga  vuttaṃ bhagavatā tiṇimāni bhikkhave asaṅkhatassa asaṅkhatalakkhaṇāni  asaṅkhatānaṃ bhikkhave dhammānaṃ na uppādo paññāyati  na vayo paññāyati  na ṭhitānaṃ aññathattaṃ paññāyatīti  puggalassa na uppādo paññāyāti  na vayo paññāyati  naṭhitassa aññathattaṃ paññāyati  tena hi puggalo asaṅkhatoti  
  
      sa  pu  parinibbuto puggalo atthatthamhi natthatthamhīti  atthatthamhiti parinibbuto puggalo sassatoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbepe 
 sa  anu  natthatthamhīti parinibbuto puggalo ucchinnoti  pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 sacchikaṭṭhasabhāvānuyogo  
  
      sa  pu  puggalo kiṃ nissāya tiṭṭhatīti  bhavaṃ nissāya tiṭaṭhatīti  
 bhavo anicco saṅkhato paṭiccasamuppanno khayadhammo vayadhammo virāgadhammo nirodhadhammo vipariṇāmadhammoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
  
    ṭhitassa  sīmu  
  
     
  
 sa  anu  puggalopi anicco saṅkato paṭiccasamuppanno khayadhammo vayadhammo virāgadhammo nirodhadhammo vipariṇāmadhammoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbepe 
  
      pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  nanu atthi koci sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno sukhaṃ vedanaṃ sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānātīti  
             
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci atthi koci sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānāti  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
      pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  nanu atthi koci dukkhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno pe 
 adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānātīti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci atthi koci adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno 
 adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānāti  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
      sa  pu  atthi koci sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno sukhaṃ vedanaṃ 
 vediyāmīti pajānātī ti katvā tena ca kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  yo sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānāti sveva puggalo  yo sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmano sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti na pajānāti na so puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
               
  
 sa  anu  yo dukkhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno pe yo adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānāti sveva puggalo  yo adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti na pajānati na so puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  atthi koci sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānātīti katvā tena ca kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭha paramatthenāti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  aññā sukhā vedanā  añño sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno sukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānātīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe sa  anu  aññā dukkhā             
 vedanā  pe aññā adukakhamasukhā vedanā  añño adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyamāno adukkhamasukhaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmīti pajānātīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  nanu atthi koci kāye kāyānupassī viharītīti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci atthi koci kāye kāyānupassī viharati  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
      pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  nanu atthi koci vedanāsu pe citte pe dhammesu dhammānupassī viharatīti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
               
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci atthi koci dhammānupassī viharatī  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
      sa  pu  atthi koci kāye kāyānupassī viharatīti katvā tena ca kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭha paramatthenāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  yo kāye kāyānupassī viharati sveva puggalo  yo na kāye kāyānupassī viharati na so puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  yo vedanāsu pe citte pe dhammesu dhammānupassī 
 viharati sveva puggalo  yo na dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati na so puggaloti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  atthi koci kāye kāyānupassī viharatīti katvā tena ca 
 kāraṇena puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  añño kāyo  añño kāye kāyānupassī viharatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
             
 sa  anu  aññā vedanā pe aññaṃ cittaṃ pe aññe dhammā  
 añño dhammesu dhammānupassī viharatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      pa  pu  puggalo nūpalabbhati   saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
  
    upalabbhati  sīmu  machasaṃ  syā      
  
               
  
 pa  anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  
 suññato lokaṃ avkkhessu 
 mogharājā   sadā sato

 evaṃ maccutaro siyā  
 evaṃ lokaṃ avekkhantaṃ 
 maccurājā na passatī ti  
 attheva suttantoti  
  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  niga  tena hi   puggalo upalabbhati saccikaṭṭhaparamatthenāti  
  
      sa  pu  puggalo avkkhetīti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  saha rūpena avkkheti   vinā rūpena avekkhatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  saha rūpena avekkhati  
 sa  anu  taṃ jīvaṃ taṃ sarīranti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  anu  saha rūpena avekkhati  vinā rūpena avekkhatīti    pa  paṭiññā  vinā rūpena avekkhati  
 sa  anu  aññaṃ jīvaṃ aññaṃ sarīranti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
      sa  pu  puggalo avekkhatīti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  abbhantaragato avekkhati  bahiddhā nikkhamitvā avekkhatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  abbhantaragato avekkhati  
 sa  anu  taṃ jīvaṃ taṃ sarīranti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe
