   pag             
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  natthi arahato satthari vimati  dhamme vimati  saṅghe vimati  sikkhāya vimati  pubbante vimati  aparante vimati  pubbantāparante vimati  idappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu vimatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci natthi arahato satthari vimati pe idappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppannesu dhammise vimati  anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  atthi ahato vimatīti  ti  
  
     sa  pu  atthi puthujjanassa vimati  atthi tassa satthari vimati pe idappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu vimatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
               
  
 sa  anu  atthi arahato vimati  atthi tassa satthari vimati pe 
 idappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu vimatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato vimati  natthi tassa satthari vimati peidappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppannosu dhamemasu vimatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi puthujjanassa vimati  natthi tassa satthari vimati pe 
 idappaccayatāpaṭicca samuppannesu dhammesu vimatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe  
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  pu  arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhi kissa nissandoti  
 pa  vi  asitapītakhāyitasāyitassa nissandoti  
 sa  pu  arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhi asitapītakhāyitasāyitassa 
 nissandoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  ye keci asanti picanti khādanti   sāyanti  
 sabbesaññeva atthi asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
              
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
     sa  pu  ye keci asanti picanti khādanti sāyanti  sabbesaññeva atthi asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  dārakā asanti picanti khādanti sāyanti  atthi dārakānaṃ asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  anu  paṇḍakā asanti pacanti khādanti sāyanti  atthi paṇḍakānaṃ asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  anu  devā asanti picanti khādanti   sāyanti  atthi devānaṃ asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
  
    khāyanti     
  
               
  
     sa  pu  arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhi asitapītakhāyitasāyitassa 
 nissandoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi tassa āsayoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  arahato uccārapassāvo asitapītakhāyitasāyitassa 
 nissando  atthi tassa āsayoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  arahato asicu sukkavisaṭṭhi asitapītakhāyitasāyitissa nissando  atthi tassa āsayoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhi asitapītakhāyitasāyitassa nissando  natthi tassa āsayoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  arahato uccārapassāvo asitapītathāyitasāyitassa nissando  natthi tassa āsayoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  arahā methunaṃ dhammaṃ paṭiseveyya  methunaṃ dhammaṃ 
 uppādeyya  puttasambādhasayanaṃ ajjhāvaseyya  kāsikacandanaṃ paccanubhaveyya  mālāgandhavilepanaṃ dhāreyya  
 jātarūparajataṃ sādiyeyyāti  
              
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  atthi puthujjanassa asuci sukkavisaṭṭhi  puthujjano methunaṃ dhammaṃ 
 paṭiseveyya  methunaṃ dhammaṃ uppādeyya  puttasambādhasayanaṃ ajjhāvaseyya  kāsikacandanaṃ paccanubhaveyya  mālāgandhavilepanaṃ dhāreyya  jātarūparajataṃ sādiyeyyāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhi  arahā methunaṃ dhammaṃ 
 paṭiseveyya  methunaṃ dhammaṃ uppādeyya  puttasambādhasayanaṃ ajjhāvaseyaya  kāyikacandanaṃ paccanubhaveyya  mālāgandhavilepanaṃ dhāreyya  jātarūparajataṃ sādiyeyyāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
               
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhi  na ca arahā methunaṃ dhammaṃ paṭiseveyya  methunaṃ dhammaṃ uppādeyya  puttasbādhasayanaṃ ajjhāvaseyya  kāsikacandanaṃ paccunubhaveyya  mālāgandhavilepanaṃ dhāreyya  jātarūparajataṃ sādiyeyyati  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi puthujjanassa asuci sukkavisaṭṭhi  na ca puthujjano methunaṃ 
 dhammaṃ paṭiseveyya  methunaṃ dhammaṃ uppādeyya  puttasambādhasayanaṃ ajjhāvaseyya  kāsikacandanaṃ paccanubhaveyya  mālāgandhavilepanaṃ dhāreyya  jātarūparajataṃ sādiyeyyati  pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  nanu arahato rāgo pahīno ucchinnamūlo tālāvatthukato 
 anabhāvakato āyatiṃ anuppādadhammoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmanatā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci arahato rāgo pahīno ucchinnamūlo tālāvatthukato 
 anabhāvakato āyatiṃ anuppādadhammo  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu arahato doso pahīno pe moho pahīno 
 pe māno pahīno pe diṭṭhī pahīnā pe vicikicchā pahīnā pethinaṃ pahīnaṃ pe middhaṃ pahīnaṃ pe uddhaccaṃ pahīnaṃ  pe ahirikaṃ pahīnaṃ pe anottappaṃ pahīnaṃ ucchinnamūlaṃ tālāvatthukataṃ anabhāvakataṃ āyatiṃ anuppādadhammanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
               
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci arahato anottappaṃ pahīnaṃ ucchinnamūlaṃ              tālāvatthukataṃ anabhāvakataṃ āyatiṃ anuppādadhammaṃ  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu arahato rāgappahānāya maggo bhāvitoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci arahato rāgappahānāya maggo bhāvito  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  atthi arahato asuci 
 sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu arahato rāgappahānāya satipaṭṭhānaṃ bhāvitā pe 
 sammappadhānā bhāvitā peiddhipādā bhāvitā pe 
 indriyā bhāvitā pe balā bhāvitā pe bojjhaṅgā bhāvitāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañcañi arahato rāgappahānāya bojjhaṅgā bhāvitā  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu arahato dosappahānāya pe mohappanāya pe 
 anottappappahānāya pe maggo bhāvito pe bojjhaṅgā bhāvitāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci arahato anottappahānāya bojjhaṅgā bhāvitā  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
  
               
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu arahā vītarāgo vītadoso vītamoho katakaraṇiyo 
 ohitabhāro anuppattasadattho parikkhīnabhavasaññojano sammadaññā vimutto ukkhittapaligho saṃkiṇṇaparikho abbuḷhesiko niraggaḷo ariyo pannadhajo pannabhāro visaññutto suvijitavijayo  dukkhaṃ tassa pariññātaṃ samudayo pahīno nirodho sacchikato maggo bhāvito  abhiññeyyaṃ abhiññātaṃ pariññeyyaṃ pariññātaṃ              pahātabbaṃ pahīnaṃ bhāvetabbaṃ bhāvitaṃ sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikatanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci arahā vītarāgo vītadoso vītamoho katakaraṇīyo 
 pe sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  vi  sadhammakusalassa arahato atthi asuci sukkavisaṭṭhi  paradhammakusalassa 
 arahato natthi asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 sa  pu  sadhammakusalassa arahato atthi asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  paradhammakusalassa arahato atthi asuca sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  paradhammakusalassa arahato natthi asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sadhammakusalassa arahato nattha asucisukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
               
  
     sa  pu  sadhammakusalassa arahato rāgo pahīno  atthi tassa asuci 
 sukkaviṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  paradhammakusalassa arahato rāgo pahīno  atthi tassa asuci 
 sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  sadhammakusalassa arahato doso pahīno pemoho 
 pahīno pe anottappaṃ pahīnaṃ  atthi tassa asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  paradhammakusalassa arahato anottappaṃ pahīnaṃ  atthi tassa 
 asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  sadhammakusalassa arahato rāgappahānāya maggo bhāvito 
 pe bojjhaṅgā bhāvitā pedosappahānāya pe mohappahānāya peanottappappahānāya maggo bhāvāto pe bojjhaṅgā bhāvitā  atthi tassa asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti               
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  paradhammakusalassa arahato anottappappahānāya bojjhaṅgā 
 bhāvitā  atthi tassa asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  sadhammakusalo araha vītarāgo vītadoso vītamoho pe sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ  atthī tassa asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  paradhammakusalo arahā vītarāgo vītadoso vītamoho 
 pe sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ  atthi tassa asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  paradhammakusalassa arahato rāgo pahīno natthi tassa asuci 
 sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sadhammakusalassa arahato rāgo pahīno  natthi tassa asuci 
 sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
               
  
     sa  pu  paradhammakusalassa arahato doso pahīno pemoho 
 pahīno pe anottappa pahīnaṃ  natthi tassa asuci sukkaviṭṭhati  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sadhammakusalassa arahato anottappaṃ pahīnaṃ  natthi tassa asuci 
 sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  paradhammakusalassa arahato rāgappahānāya maggo bhāvito 
 pe bojjhaṅgā bhāvitā pedosappahānāya pe mohappahānāya peanottappappahānāya maggo bhāvito pe bojjhaṅgā bhāvitā  natthi tassa asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sadhammakusalassa arahato anottappappahānāya bojjhaṅgā 
 bhāvitā  natthi tassa asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbepe 
  
     sa  pu  paradhammakusalo arahā vītarāgo vītadoso vītamoho 
 pe sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ  natthi tassa asuci sukkavisaṭṭhīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā               
 sa  anu  sadhammakusalo arahā vītarāgo vītadoso vītamoho 
 pe sacchikātābbaṃ sacchikataṃ  natthi tassa asuci sukkavasiṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā ye keci bhikkhave bhikkhu puthujjanā 
 sīlasampannā satā sampajānā niddaṃ okkamanti  tesaṃ asuci na muccati  ye pi te bhikkhave  bāhirakā isayo kāmesu vītarāgā  tesampi asuci na muccati  aṭṭhāna metaṃ bhikkhave  anavakāso yaṃ arahato asuci mucceyayāti  a   attheva suttantoti  
  
  
  a   mahāvaggapāḷiyaṃ cīvarakkhandhake nisīdanānuññātakathā samannābharitabbā  
  
               
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ  atthi arahato asuci sukkavisaṭṭhiti  
  
     pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ atthi arahato parūpahāroti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  nanu arahato 
 cīvarapiṇḍapātasenāsanagilānapaccayabhesajjaparikkhāraṃ pare upasaṃhareyyunti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  anu  ṭha  hañci arahato cīvarapiṇḍapātasenāsanagilānapaccayabhesajjaparikkhāraṃ pare upasaṃhareyyuṃ  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe atthi arahato parūpaharoti  
     sa  pu  arahato cīvarapiṇḍapātasenāsanagilānapaccayabhesajjaparikkhāraṃ pare upasaṃhareyyunti atthī arahato parūpahāroti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  arahato sotāpattiphalaṃ vā sakadāgāmiphalaṃ vā anāgāmiphalaṃ vā arahattaṃ vā pare upasaṃhareyyunti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 parūpahārakathā              niṭṭhitā  
  
               
  
       
 aññāṇakathā  
  
    sa  pu  atthi arahato aññāṇantā  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi arahato avijjā avijjogho avijjāyogo avijjānusayo avijjāpariyuṭṭhānaṃ avijjāsaññojanaṃ avijjānīvaraṇanti  pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  pu  natthi arahato avijjā avijjogho avijjāyogo avijjānusayo avijjāpariyuṭṭhānaṃ avijjāsaññojanaṃ avijjānīvaraṇanti  pa  paṭiññā āmantā  anu  ṭha  hañci natthi arahato avijjā avijjogho avijjāyogo avijjānusayo avijjāpariyuṭṭhānaṃ avijjāsaññojanaṃ avijjānīvaraṇaṃ  anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe atthi arahato aññāṇanti  
  
    sa  pu  atthi puthujjanassa aññāṇaṃ  atthi tassa 
 avijjā avijjogho avijjāyogo avijjānusayo avijjāpariyuṭṭhānaṃ avijjāsaññojanaṃ avijjānīvaraṇanti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi arahato aññāṇaṃ  atthi tassa avijjā avijjogho 
 avijjāyogo avijjānusayo avijjāpariyuṭṭhānaṃ avijjāsaññojanaṃ avijjajānīvaraṇanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  atthi avijjāyogo avijjānusayo avijjāpariyuṭṭhānaṃ avijjāsaññojanaṃ avijjānīvaraṇanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi puthujjanassa aññāṇaṃ  natthi tassa avijjā avijjogho avijjāyogo avijjānusayo avijjāpariyuṭṭhānaṃ avijjāsaññojanaṃ avijjānīvaraṇanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
               
  
    sa  pu  atthi arahato aññāṇanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  arahā aññāṇāpakato pāṇaṃ haneyya  adinnaṃ ādiyeyya 
 musā bhaṇeyya  pisuṇaṃ bhaṇeyya  pharusaṃ bhaṇeyaya  samphaṃ palapeyya   sandhiṃ chindeyaya  nilopaṃ hareyya  ekāgārikaṃ kareyya  paripanthe tiṭṭheyaya  paradāraṃ gaccheyya  gāmaghātaṃ kareyya  nigamaghātaṃ kareyyā ti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  atthi puthujjanassa aññāṇaṃ  puthujjano aññāṇāpakato              pāṇaṃ  haneyya adinnaṃ ādiyeyya  musā bhaṇeyya pe gāmaghātaṃ kareyaya  nigamaghātaṃ kāreyyāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi arahato aññāṇaṃ  arahā aññāṇāpakato pāṇaṃ 
 haneyya  adinnaṃ ādiyeyya pegāmaghātaṃ kareyya  nigamaghātaṃ kareyyāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  atthi arahato aññāṇaṃ  na ca arahā aññāṇāpakato pāṇaṃ haneyya  adinnaṃ ādiyeyya pegāmaghātaṃ kareyya  nigamaghātaṃ kareyyāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi puthujjanassa aññāṇaṃ  na ca puthujjano aññāṇāpakato 
 pāṇaṃ haneyya  adinnaṃ ādiyeyyapegāmaghātaṃ kareyya  nigamaghātaṃ kareyyāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  atthi arahato aññāṇanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi arahato satthari aññāṇaṃ dhamme aññāṇaṃ saṅghe 
 aññāṇaṃ sikkhāya aññāṇaṃ pubbante aññāṇaṃ aparante aññāṇaṃ pubbantāparante aññāṇaṃ idapaccayatā paṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu aññāṇanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
    samphapapalāpeyya    
  
               
  
    sa  pu  natthi arahato satthari aññāṇaṃ  dhamme aññāṇaṃ 
 saṅghe aññāṇaṃ  sikkhāya aññāṇaṃ  pubbante aññāṇaṃ  aparante aññāṇaṃ  pubbantāparante aññāṇaṃ  idappaccayatā paṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu aññāṇanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci natthi arahato satthari aññāṇaṃ  dhamme aññāṇaṃ  
 saṅghe aññāṇaṃ pe idappaccayatā paṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu aññāṇaṃ  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  atthi arahato aññāṇanti  
  
     sa  pu  atthi puthujjanassa aññāṇaṃ  atthi tassa satthari aññāṇaṃ  
 dhamme aññāṇaṃ  saṅghe aññāṇaṃ  peidappaccayatā paṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu aññāṇanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi arahato aññāṇaṃ  atthi tassa satthari aññāṇaṃ  dhamme aññāṇaṃ  saṅghe aññāṇaṃ  peidappaccayatā paṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu aññāṇanti               
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe

 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā

    jānatvāhaṃ  sīmu  sya    
  a   khandhasaṃyutta  vāsijaṭasutta  
  b   saccasaṃyutta  āsavakkhayasutta  
  
               
  
 sa  anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  
  
  onemissing  yadā have pātubhavanti dhammā 
 ātāpino jhāyato brāhmaṇassa  
 athassa kaṅkhā vapayanti sabbā 
 yato pajānāti sahetudhammanti  
  
 yadā have pātu bhavanti dhammā 
 ātāpino jhāyato brāhmaṇassa  
 athassa kaṅkhā vapayanti sabbā  
 yato khayaṃ paccayānaṃ avedīti  
  
 yadā have pātubhavanti dhammā 
 ātāpino jhāyato brāhmaṇassa  
 vidhūpayaṃ tiṭṭhati mārasenaṃ 
 suriyova obhāsayamantaḷikkhanti   a   
  
 yā kāci kaṅkhā idha vā huraṃ vā 
 sakavediyā vā paravedayā vā  
 jhāyino tā pajahanti sabbā 
              ātāpino brahmacariyaṃ varantāti   b   
  
 ye kaṅkhā samatikkantā 
 kaṅkhā bhutesu pāṇisu  
 asaṃsayā visaṃyuttā 
 tesu dinnaṃ mahapphalanti  
  
 etādisī dhammapakāsanettha 
 na tattha kiṃ   kaṅkhati koci sāvako  
 nittiṇṇaoghaṃ   vicikicchachinnaṃ  
 buddhaṃ namassāma jinaṃ janindanti      c   
  
 attheva suttantoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ atthi arahato kaṅkhāti  
  
  
  
  a   mahāvaggapāḷi  udānapāḷi  bodhisutta 
  b   udāna pāḷi  revatasutta  
    kinnu tattha kaṅkhati     syā  
    tiṇṇaoghaṃ  sīmu     
    janindāti  sīmu      machasaṃ  
    dīghanikāya  sakkapañhasutta 
  
               
  
     pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ atthi arahato kaṅkhāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  nanu arahā itthipurisānaṃ nāmagotte kaṅkheyya  maggāmagge 
 kaṅkheyya  tiṇakaṭṭhavanappatīnaṃ nāme kaṅkheyyāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci arahā itthipurisānaṃ nāmagotte kaṅkheyya  maggāmagge kaṅkheyaya  tiṇakaṭṭhavanappatīnaṃ nāme kaṅkheyya  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe atthi arahato kaṅkhāti  
  
     sa  pu  arahā itthipurisānaṃ nāmagotte kaṅkheyyaṃ  maggāmagge 
 kaṅkheyya  tiṇakaṭṭhavanappatīnaṃ nāme kaṅkhyoti atthi arahato kaṅkheyyāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  arahā sotāpattiphale vā sakadāgāmiphale vā anāgāmi phale 
 vā arahatte vā kaṅkheyyāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 kaṅkhākathā              niṭṭhitā  
  
               
  
       
  
 paravitaraṇakathā   
  
    sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti     
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  arahā paraneyyo parapattiyo parapaccayo parapaṭibaddhabhu na 
 jānāti na passati samumūḷho asampajānoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  anu  nanu arahā na paraneyeyā na parapattiyo na parapaṭibaddhibhra 
 jānāti passati asammuḷho sampajānoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci arahā na paraneyyo na parapattiyo na parapaccayo 
 na parapaṭibaddhabhu jānāti passati asammūḷho sampajāno  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
  
    sa  pu  atthi puthujanassa paravitaraṇā  so ca paraneyyo parapattiyo 
 parapattiyo parapaccayo parapaṭibaddhabhu  na jānāti na passatī sammuḷho asampajānoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthī arahato paravitaraṇā  so ca paraneyyā parapattiyo 
 parapattiyo parapaccayo parapaṭibaddhabhu na jānāti na passati sammūḷho asampajānoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    paravitāraṇakathā  sīmu  machasaṃ      syā  
    paravitaraṇāti  sīmu  machasaṃ      syā  
  
               
  
    sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇā  so ca na paraneyyo na 
 parapattiyo na parapaccayo na parapaṭipaddhabhū jānāti passati asammūḷho sampajānoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi puthujjanassa paravitaraṇā so ca na paraneyyo na 
 parapattiyo na parapaṭibaddhabhu jānāti passati asammūḷho sampajānoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi arahato satthari paravitaraṇā  dhamme paravitaraṇṛ saṅghe 
 paravitaraṇā sikkhāya paravitaraṇā pubbante paravitaraṇā aparante paravitaraṇā pubbantāparante paravitaraṇā idappaccayatapaṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu paravitaraṇṛti               
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  anu  natthi arahato satthari paravitaraṇā dhamme paravitaraṇā pe 
 idappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe sa  anu  natthi arahato satthiri paravitaraṇā dhamme paravitaraṇā pe 
 idappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci natthi arahato satthari paravitaraṇā dhamme paravitaraṇā peidappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppannosu dhammesu paravitaraṇā  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
  
    sa  pu  atthi puthujjanassa paravitaraṇā  atthi tassa satthari paravitaraṇā 
 dhamme paravitaraṇā peidappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
               
  
 sa  anu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇā  atthi tassa satthari paravitaraṇā  
 dhamme paravitaraṇā peidappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
    sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇā  natthi tassa satthari paravitaraṇā  dhamme paravitaraṇā peidappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi puthujjanassa paravitaraṇā  natthi tassa satthari paravitaraṇā dhamme paravitaraṇā peidappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppannesu dhammesu paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
    sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu arahato rāgo pahīno ucchinnamūlo tālāvatthukato 
 anabhāvakato āyatiṃ anuppādadhammoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci arahato rāgo pahīno ucchinnamūlo tālāvatthukato 
 anabhāvakato āyatiṃ anuppādadhammo  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti               
  
    sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu arahato doso pahīno pe moho pahīno 
 anottappaṃ pahīnasaṃ ucchinnamūlaṃ tālāvatthukataṃ anabhāvakataṃ āyatiṃ anuppādadhammanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
               
  
 anu  ṭha  hañci arahato anottappaṃ pahīnaṃ ucchinnamūlaṃ tālāvatthukataṃ anabhāvakataṃ āyatiṃ anuppādadhammaṃ  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
  
    sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu arahato rāgappahānāya maggo bhāvito pe 
 bojjhaṅghā bhāvitā pedosappahānāya pe anottappappahānāya maggo bhāvito pe bojjhaṅgā bhāvitāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci arahato rāgpahānāya bojjhaṅgā bhāvitā  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu arahā vītarāgo vītadoso vītamoho pe 
 sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikatanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci arahā vītarāgo vītadoso vītamoho pe 
 sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  vi  sadhammakusalassa arahato atthi paravitaraṇā  paradhammakusalassa 
 arahato natthi paravitaraṇāti  
 sa  anu  paradhammakusalassa arahato atthi paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
               
  
 sa  anu  paradhammakusalassa arahato natthi paravitaraṇāti               
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sadhammakusalassa arahato natthi paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  sadhammakusalassa arahato rāgo pahīno atthi tassa 
 paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  paradhammakusalassa arahato rāgo pahīno atthi tassa 
 paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
     sa  pu  sadhammakusalassa arahato doso pahīno  moho pahīno 
 pe anottappaṃ pahīnaṃ  atthi tassa paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  paradhammakusalassa arahato anottappaṃ pahīnaṃ  atthi tassa 
 paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
     sa  pu  sadhammakusalassa arahato rāgappahānāya maggo bhavito pe 
 bojjhaṅgābhāvitā  atthi tassa paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  paradhammakusalassa arahato rāgappahānāya maggo bhāvito 
 pe bojjhaṅgā bhāvita  atthi tassa paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
     sa  pu  sadhammakusalassa arahato dosappahānāya pe 
 anottappappahānāya maggo bhāvito pe bojjhaṅgā bhāvitā  atthi tassa paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  paradhammakusalassa arahato anottappappahānāya bojjhaṅgā 
 bhāvitā  atthi tassa paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
               
  
     sa  pu  sadhammakusalo arahā vītarāgo vītadoso vītamoho 
 pe sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ  atthi tassa paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  paradhammakusalo arahā vītarāgo vītadoso vītamoho 
 pe sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ natthi tassa paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
                  sa  pu  paradhammakusalassa arahato rāgo pahīno  natthi tassa 
 paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sadhammakusalassa arahato rāgo pahīno  natthi tassa 
 paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
     sa  pu  paradhammakusalassa arahato doso pahīno  pe 
 anottappaṃ pahīnaṃ  natthi tassa paravitaraṇāti  
 sa  anu  sadhammakusalassa arahato doso pahīno  moho pahīno pe anottappaṃ pahīnaṃ  natthi tassa paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
     sa  pu  paradhammakusalassa arahato rāgappahānāya maggo bhāvito pe bojjhaṅgā bhāvitā pe dosappahānāya peanottappappahānāya maggo bhāvito pe bojjhaṅgā bhāvitā natthi tassa paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sadhammakusalassa arahato anottappappahānāya bojjhaṅgā bhāvitā  natthi tassa paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
     sa  pu  paradhammakusalo arahā vītarāgo  vītadoso vītamoho 
 pe sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ  natthi tassa paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
               
  
 sa  anu  sadhammakusalo arahā vītarāgo  vītadoso  vītamoho pe sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ  natthi tassa paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
     sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā jānatohaṃ   bhikkhave passato āsavānaṃ khayaṃdāmi  no ajānato no apassato  kiñca bhikkhave jānato kiṃ passato āsavānaṃ khayo hoti iti rūpaṃ pe iti viññāṇassa atthaṅgamoti  evaṃ kho bhikkhave jānato evaṃ passato āsavānaṃ khayo hotīti   a  attheva suttantoti               
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā jānatohaṃ bhikkhave passato 
 āsavānaṃ khayaṃ vadāmi  no ajānato no apassato  kiñca bhikkhave jānato kiṃ passato āsavānaṃ khayo hoti idaṃ dukkhanti bhikkhave jānato passato āsavānaṃ khayo hoti  ayaṃ dukkhasamudayoti pe ayaṃ dukkhanirodhotipe ayaṃ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadāti jānato passato āsavānaṃ khayo hotīti   b  attheva suttantoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
  
    jānatvāhaṃ  sīmu  
  a   khandhasaṃyutta  vāsijaṭasutta  
  b   saccasaṃyutta  āsavakkhayasutta 
  
               
  
 sa  anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā sabbaṃ bhikkhave anabhijānaṃ aparijānaṃ avirājayaṃ appajahaṃ abhabbo dukkhakkhayāya peidaṃ kho bhikkhave   abhijānaṃ parijānaṃ virājayaṃ pajahaṃ bhabbo  dukkhakkhayāyāti   a  attheva suttantoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  
 sahāvassa dassanasampadāya pe 
 cha cābhiṭhānāni abhabbo kātunti  
 attheva suttantoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā               
 anu  pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā yasmiṃ bhikkhave samaye ariyasāvakassa 
 virajaṃ vītamalaṃ dhammacakkhuṃ udapādi yaṃ kiñci samudayadhammaṃ sabbaṃ taṃ nirodhadhammanti  sahadassanuppādā bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa tīṇi saññojanāni pahīyanti  sakkāyadiṭṭhi vicikicchā sīlabbataparāmāsoti attheva suttantoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
  
  
    sabbañca kho bhikkhave  machasaṃ  
 saḷāyatanasaṃyutta  aparijānanasuttaṃ  
  
               
  
     sa  pu  atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā 
  
 nāhaṃ sahissāmi   pamocanāya 
 kathākathiṃ   dhotaka kañci loke  
 dhammañca seṭṭhaṃ abhijānamāno 
 evaṃ tuvaṃ oghamimaṃ taresīti   a   
 attheva suttantoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
  
     pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  nanu arahato ittipurisānaṃ nāmagottaṃ pare vitareyyuṃ   
 maggāmaggaṃ pare vitareyyuṃ     tiṇakaṭṭhavanappatīnaṃ nāmaṃ pare vitareyyunti     
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci arahato itthi purisānaṃ nāmagottaṃ pare vitareyyuṃ  
 maggāmaggaṃ pare vitareyyuṃ  tiṇakaṭṭhavanappatīnaṃ              nāmaṃ pare vitareyyuṃ  anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
  
     sa  pu  arahato itthipurisānaṃ nāmagottaṃ pare vitareyyuṃ  maggāmaggaṃ pare vitareyyuṃ  tiṇakaṭṭhavanappatīnaṃ nāmaṃ pare vitareyyunti atthi arahato paravitaraṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  arahato sotāpattiphalaṃ vā sakadāgāmiphalaṃ vā 
 anāgāmiphalaṃ vā arahattaṃ   vā pare vitareyyunti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 paravitaraṇakathā niṭṭhitā  
  
  
  
    gamissāmi  sīmu     
    kathaṃkathi  sīmu  
    vitāreyyuṃ  sīmu  machasaṃ  syā     
    arahattaphalaṃ vā  sīmu  
  a   suttanipāte  dhotakasuttaṃ 
  
               
  
       
  
 vacībhedakathā  
  
    sa  pu  samāpannassa atthi vacībhedoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sabbattha samāpannānaṃ atthi vacībhedoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
    sa  pu  samāpannassa atthi vacībhedoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sabbadā samāpannānaṃ atthi vacībhedoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
    sa  pu  samāpannassa atthi vacībhedoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sabbesaṃ samāpannānaṃ atthi vacībhedoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
    sa  pu  samāpannassa atthi vacībhedoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sabbasamāpattīsu atthi vacībhedoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe    sa  pu  samāpannassa atthi vacībhedoti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  sa  anu  samāpannassa atthi kāyabhedoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
              
               
  
    sa  pu  samāpannassa natthi kāyabhedoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  samāpannassa natthi vacībhedoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  samāpānnassa atthi vācā  atthi vacībhedoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  samāpannassa atthi kāyo  atthi kāyabhedoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  samāpannassa atthi kāyo  natthi kāyabhedoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  samāpannassa atthi vācā  natthi vacībhedoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  dukkhanti jānanto dukkhanti vācaṃ bhāsatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  samudayoti jānanto samudayoti vācaṃ bhāsatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  dukkhanti jānanto dukkhanti vācaṃ bhāsatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nirodhoti jānanto nirodhoti vācaṃ bhāsatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  dukkhanti jānanto dukkhanti vācaṃ bhāsatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  maggoti jānanto maggoti vācaṃ bhāsatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  samudayoti jānanto na ca samudayoti vāca bhāsatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  dukkhanti jānanto na ca dukkhanti vācaṃ bhāsatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
                  sa pu  nirodhoti jānanto na ca nirodhoti vācaṃ bhāsatīti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa anu  dukkhanti jānanto na ca dukkhanti vācaṃ bhāsatīti  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbo pe

 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe

 sa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā sikhissa ānaṇda bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddassa  ahibhu nāma sāvako brahmaloke ṭhito dasasahassīlokadhātuṃ sarena viññāpesi  a  
 ārabhatha nikkhamatha yuñjata buddhasāsane 
 dhunātha maccuno senaṃ naḷāgāraṃ ca kuñjaro yo imasmiṃ dhammavinaye appamatto vihessati  
 pahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ dukkhassantaṃ karissatīti  b  
 attheva suttantoti  sa paṭiññā  āmantā  anu pā  tena hi samāpannassa atthi vacībhedoti

 dukkhāhārakathā  
  
   sa pu  dukkhāhāro maggaṅgaṃ maggapariyāpannanti               
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa anu  ye keci dukkhanti vācaṃ bhāsanti  sabbe te maggaṃ bhāventīti  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
   sa pu  ye keci dukkhanti vācaṃ bhāsanti  sabbe te maggaṃ bhāventīti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa anu  bālaputhujjanā dukkhanti vācaṃ bhāsanti  bālaputhujjanā maggaṃ bhāventīti  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa anu  mātughātako pe pitughātako pe arahantaghātako pelohituppādako pe saṅghabhedako dukkhanti vācaṃ bhāsati  saṅghabhedako maggaṃ bhāvetīti  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 dukkhāhārakathā niṭṭhitā  
  
                 
  
 cittaṭṭhitikathā  
  
   sa pu  ekaṃ cittaṃ divasaṃ tiṭṭhatīti

 sa anu  upaḍḍhadivaso uppādakkhaṇo  upaḍḍhadivaso vayakkhaṇoti

   sa pu  ekaṃ cittaṃ dve divase tiṭṭhatīti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa anu  divaso uppādakkhaṇo  divaso vayakkhaṇoti  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe

 dve kappasahassāni tiṭṭhati pe cattāri kappasahassāni tiṭṭhati pe aṭṭha kappasahassāni tiṭṭhati pe soḷasa kappasahassāni tiṭṭhati pe vīsati kappasahassāni tiṭṭhati pecattārīsa kappasahassāni tiṭṭhati pe saṭṭhi kappasahassāni tiṭṭhati pecaturāsīti kappasahassāni tiṭṭhatīti

 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  ekaṃ cittaṃ divasaṃ tiṭṭhatīti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa pu  atthaññe dhammā ekāhaṃ bahumpi uppajjitvā nirujjhantīti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa anu  te dhammā cittena lahuparivattāti  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  te dhammā cittena lahuparivattāti  
 pa paṭññā  āmantā  
 sa anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā nāhaṃ bhikkhave  aññaṃ ekadhammampi samanupassāmi yaṃ evaṃ lahuparivattaṃ  yathayidaṃ cittaṃ  yāvañcidaṃ bhikkhave  upamāpi na sukarā yāva lahuparivattaṃ cittanti a  attheva suttantoti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ te dhammā cittena lahuparivattāti

 sa anu  cakkhuviññāṇaṃ divasaṃ tiṭṭhatīti  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
  a   ekaka aṅguttara  pañcamavagga  
  
                 
  
 sa anu  sotaviññāṇaṃ pe ghānaviññāṇaṃ pejivhāviññāṇaṃ pekāyaviññāṇaṃ pe akusalacittaṃ perāgasahagataṃ pedosasahagataṃ pemohasahagataṃ pemānasahagataṃ pediṭṭhisahagataṃ pe vicikicchāsahagataṃ pethīnasahagataṃ peuddhaccasahagataṃ pe ahirikasahagataṃ peanottappasahagataṃ cittaṃ divasaṃ tiṭṭhatīti  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
    sa pu  ekaṃ cittaṃ divasaṃ tiṭṭhatīti  pa paṭiññā  āmantā  sa anu  yeneva cittena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati  teneva cittena sotena saddaṃ suṇāti  pe ghānena gaṇdhaṃ ghāyati pejivhāya rasaṃ sāyati pe kāyena phoṭṭhabbaṃ phusati pemanasā dhammaṃ vijānāti pe yeneva cittena manasā dhammaṃ vijānāti  teneva cittena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati pesotena saddaṃ suṇāti pe ghānena gaṇdhaṃ ghāyati pejivhāya rasaṃ sāyati pe kāyena phoṭṭhabbaṃ phusatīti  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  ekaṃ cittaṃ divasaṃ tiṭṭhatīti

 kukkuḷakathā  
  
    sa pu  sabbe saṅkhārā anodhiṃ katvā  kukkuḷāti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa anu  nanu atthi sukhā vedanā  kāyikaṃ sukhaṃ cetasikaṃ              sukhaṃ dibbaṃ sukhaṃ mānusakaṃ sukhaṃ lābhasukhaṃ  sakkārasukhaṃ yānasukhaṃ sayanasukhaṃ issariyasukhaṃ ādhipaccasukhaṃ  gihīsukhaṃ sāmaññasukhaṃ sāsavaṃ sukhaṃ anāsavaṃ sukhaṃ upadhisukhaṃ nirupadhisukhaṃ sāmisaṃ sukhaṃ nirāmisaṃ sukhaṃ sappītikaṃ sukhaṃ nippītikaṃ sukhaṃ jhānasukhaṃ vimuttisukhaṃ kāmasukhaṃ nekkhammasukhaṃ pavivekasukhaṃ  upasamasukhaṃ sambodhasukhanti   
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu ṭha  hañci atthi sukhā vedanā kāyikaṃ sukhaṃ pesambodhasukhaṃ   
 anu pā  no ca vata re vattabbe sabbe saṅkhārā anodhiṃ katvā kukkuḷāti  
  
    sa pu  sabbe saṃkhārā anodhiṃ katvā  kukkuḷāti

    adhipaccasukhaṃ  sīmu

    sambodhisukhaṃ      
    ādittā  sīmu  
  
                 
 pa anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavataṃ sabbaṃ bhikkhave ādittaṃ  kiñci bhikkhave  sabbaṃ ādittaṃ  cakkhuṃ bhikkhave ādittaṃ  rūpā ādittā  cakkhuviññāṇaṃ ādittaṃ  cakkhusamphasso āditto  yampidaṃ cakkhusamphassapaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṃ sukhaṃ vā dukkhaṃ vā adukkhamasukhaṃ vā tampi ādittaṃ  kena ādittaṃ  rāgagginā dosagginā mohagginā ādittaṃ  jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi ādittanti vadāmi  sotaṃ ādittaṃ  saddā ādittā peghānaṃ ādittaṃ  gaṇdhā ādittā pe jivhā ādittā  rasā ādittā pekāyo āditto  phoṭṭhabbā ādittā pe mano āditto  dhammā ādittā pe mano viññāṇaṃ ādittaṃ  manosamphasso āditto  yampidaṃ  manosamphassappaccayā uppajjati vedayitaṃ sukhaṃ vā dukkhaṃ vā adukkhamasukhaṃ vā tampi ādittaṃ  kena ādittaṃ  rāgagginā dosagginā mohagginā ādittaṃ  jātiyā jarāya maraṇena sokehi paridevehi dukkhehi domanassehi upāyāsehi ādittanti vadāmī a ti attheva suttantoti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
              anu pā  tena hi sabbe saṅkhārā anodhiṃ katvā kukkuḷāti  
  
    sa pu  sabbe saṅkhārā anodhiṃ katvā kukkuḷāti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā pañcime bhikkhave kāmaguṇā  katame pañca  cakkhu viññeyyā rūpā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṃhitā rajanīyā  sota viññeyyā saddā peghānaviññeyyā gaṇdhā pe jivhāviññeyyā rasā pekāyaviññeyyā phoṭṭhabbā iṭṭhā kantā manāpā piyarūpā kāmūpasaṃhitā rajanīyā  ime kho bhikkhave pañcakāmaguṇāti b  attheva suttantoti

 anu pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ  sabbe saṅkhārā anodhiṃ katvā kukkuḷāti  
  
    yamidaṃ  machasaṃ  
  a   saḷāyatanasaṃyutta  sabbavagga  ādittasutta  
  b   majjhimanikāya  mahādukkhakkhaṇdhasutta  
  
                 
    pa pu  na vattabbaṃ  sabbe saṅkhārā anodhi katvā kukkuḷāti  
 sa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā lābhā vo bhikkhave suladdhaṃ vo bhikkhave  khaṇo vo paṭiladdho  brahmacariyāvāsāya  diṭṭhā mayā bhikkhave cha phassāyatanikā nāma nirayā  tattha yaṃ kiñci cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati aniṭṭharūpaññeva passati no iṭṭharūpaṃ  akantarūpaññeva passati no kantarūpaṃ  amanāparūpaññeva passati no manāparūpaṃ  yaṃ kiñci sotena saddaṃ suṇāti pe ghānena gaṇdhaṃ ghāyati pe jivhāya rasaṃ sāyati pekāyena phoṭṭhabbaṃ phusati pe manasā dhammaṃ vijānāti  aniṭṭharūpaññeva vijānāti no iṭṭharūpaṃ  akantarūpaññeva vijānāti nokantarūpaṃ  amanāparūpaññeva vijānāti no manāparūpanti a  attheva suttantoti

    sa pu  sabbe saṅkhārā anodhiṃ katvā kukkuḷāti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā lābhā vo bhikkhave  suladdhaṃ vo bhikkhave  khaṇo vo paṭiladdho brahmacariyavāsāya  diṭṭhā mayā bhikkhave cha phassāyatanikā              nāma saggā  tattha yaṃ kiñci cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati iṭṭharūpaññeva passati no aniṭṭharūpaṃ  kantarūpaññeva passati no akantarūpaṃ  manāparūpaññeva passati no amanāparūpaṃ  yaṃ kiñci sotena saddaṃ suṇāti pe ghānena gaṇdhaṃ ghāyati pe jivhāya rasaṃ ghāyati pe 
  
    paṭividdho      
  a   saḷāyatanasaṃyutta  devadahavagga khaṇasutta  
  
                 
 kāyena phoṭṭhabbaṃ phusati pe manasā dhammaṃ vijānāti  iṭṭharūpaññeva vijānāti no aniṭṭharūpaṃ  kantarūpaññeva vijānāti no akantarūpaṃ  manāparūpaññeva vijānāti no amanāparūpanti  a  attheva suttantoti

    sa pu  sotipattiphalasacchikiriyāpaṭipanno puggalo dukkhadassanena kiṃ jahatīti  
  
 pa vi  sakkāyadiṭṭhiṃ vicikicchaṃ sīlabbataparāmāsaṃ tadekaṭṭhe ca kilese catubhāgaṃ jahatīti  
 sa anu  catubhāgaṃ sotāpanno  catubhāgaṃ na sotāpanno  catubhāgaṃ sotāpattiphalappattopaṭiladdho adhigato              sacchikato upasampajja viharati  kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ na kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ sattakkhattuparamo kolaṃkolo ekabījī  buddhe aveccappasādane samannāgato dhamme pesaṅghe pe ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgatoti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
   sa pu  samudayadassanena pe nirodhadassanena pemaggadassanena kiṃ jahatīti  
  
 pa vi  sakkāyadiṭṭhiṃ vicikicchaṃ sīlabbataparāmāsaṃ tadekaṭṭhe ca kilese catubhāgaṃ jahatīti  
  
 sa anu  catubhāgaṃ sotāpanno  catubhāgaṃ na sotāpanno  catubhāgāgaṃ sotāpattiphalappatto paṭiladdho adhigato sacchikato upasampajja viharati  kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ na kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ sattakkhattuparamo kolaṃkolo ekabījī  buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato dhamme pe saṅghe pe ariyakantahi sīlehi samannāgato catubhāgaṃ na ariyakantehi sīlehi samannāgatoti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
                 
  
   sa pu  sakadāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo dukkhadassanena kiṃ jahatīti  
 pa vi  oḷārikaṃ kāmarāgaṃ oḷārikaṃ byāpādaṃ tadekaṭṭhe ca kilese catubhāgaṃ jahatīti  
  
 sa anu  catubhāgaṃ sakadāgāmī catubhāgaṃ na sakadāgāmī  catubhāgaṃ sakadāgāmiphalappatto paṭiladdho adhigato sacchikato upasampajja viharati  kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ na kāyena phusitvā viharatīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
   sa pu  samudayadassanena pe nirodhadassanena pemaggadassanena kiṃ jahatīti  
  
 pa vi  oḷārikaṃ kāmarāgaṃ oḷārikaṃ byāpādaṃ tadekaṭṭhe ca kilese catubhāgaṃ jahatīti  
  
 sa anu  catubhāgaṃ sakadāgāmī  catubhāgaṃ na sakadāgāhī  catubhāgaṃ sakadāgāmiphalappatto paṭiladdho adhigato              sacchikato upasampajja viharati  kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ na kāyena phusitvā viharatīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
   sa pu  anāgāmiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo dukkhadassanena kiṃ jahatīti  
  
 pa vi  anusahagataṃ kāmarāgaṃ aṇusahagataṃ byāpādaṃ tadekaṭṭhe ca kilese catubhāgaṃ jahatīti  
 sa anu  catubhāgaṃ anāgāmī  catubhāgaṃ na anāgāmī  catubhāgaṃ anāgāmiphalappatto paṭiladdho adhigato sacchikato upasampajja viharati  kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ na kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ antarāparinibbāyī pe upahaccaparinibbāyī peasaṅkhāraparinibbāyī pe sasaṅkhāraparinibbāyī peuddhaṃsoto akaṇiṭṭhagāmī  catubhāgaṃ na uddhaṃsoto akaṇiṭṭhagāmīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattebbe pe 
  
                 
  
    sa pu  samudayadassanena pe nirodhadassanena pemaggadassanena kiṃ jahatīti  
  
 pa vi  aṇusahagataṃ kāmarāgaṃ aṇusahagataṃ byāpādaṃ tadekaṭṭhe ca kilese catubhāgaṃ jahatīti  
 sa anu  catubhāgaṃ anāgāmī  catubhāgaṃ na anāgāmī  catubhāgaṃ anāgāmiphalappatto paṭiladdho adhigato sacchikato upasampajja viharati  kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ na kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ antarāparinibbāyī pe upahaccaparinibbāyī peasaṅkhāraparinibbāyī pe sasaṅkhāraparinibbāyī peuddhaṃsoto akaṇiṭṭhagāmī  catubhāgaṃ na uddhaṃsoto akaṇiṭṭhagāmīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  arahattaphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo dukkhadassanena kiṃ jahatīti  
  
 pa vi  rūparāgaṃ arūparāgaṃ mānaṃ uddhaccaṃ avijjaṃ tadekaṭṭhe ca kilese catubhāgaṃ jahatīti  
  
 sa anu  catubhāgaṃ arahā  catubhāgaṃ na arahā  catubhāgaṃ arahattappatto paṭiladdho adhigato sacchikato upasampajja viharati  kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ na              kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ vītarāgo pe vītadoso pevītamoho pekatakaraṇīyo ohitabhāro anuppattasadattho parikkhīṇabhavasaññojano sammadaññāvimutto ukkhittapaligho saṅkhiṇṇaparikho abbūḷhesiko niraggaḷo ariyopannaddhajo pannabhāro visaññutto suvijitavijayo  dukkhaṃ tassa pariññātaṃ samudayo pahīno nirodho sacchikato maggo bhāvito  abhiññeyyaṃ abhiññātaṃ pariññeyyaṃ pariññātaṃ pahātabbaṃ pahīnaṃ bhāvetabbaṃ bhāvitaṃ pe sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ  catubhāgaṃ sacchikātabbaṃ na sacchikatanti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattebbe pe 
  
                 
  
    sa pu  samudayadassanena pe nirodhadassanena pemaggadassanena kiṃ jahatīti  
  
 pa vi  rūparāgaṃ arūparāgaṃ mānaṃ uddhaccaṃ avijjaṃ tadekaṭṭhe ca kilese catubhāgaṃ jahatītī  
 sa anu  catubhāgaṃ arahā  catubhāgaṃ na arahā  catubhāgaṃ arahattappatto paṭiladdho adhigato sacchikato upasampajja viharati  kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ na kāyena phusitvā viharati  catubhāgaṃ vītarāgo pe vītadoso pevītamoho pe katakaraṇīyo ohitabhāro anuppattasadattho parikkhīṇabhavasaññojano sammadaññāvimutto ukkhittapaligho saṃkiṇṇaparikho abubūḷhesiko niraggaḷo ariyopannaddhajo pannahāro visaññutto suvijitavijayo  dukkhaṃ tassa pariññātaṃ samudayo pahīno nirodho sacchikato maggo bhāvito  abhiññeyyaṃ abhiññātaṃ pariññeyyaṃ pariññātaṃ pahātabbaṃ pahīnaṃ bhāvetabbaṃ bhāvitaṃ pe sacchikātabbaṃ sacchikataṃ  catubhāgaṃ sacchikātabbaṃ na sacchikatanti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  sotāpattiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo dukkhaṃ dakkhanto paṭipannakoti vattabboti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa anu  dukkhe diṭṭhe  phale ṭhitoti vattabbeti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 sa pu  samudayaṃ dakkhanto pe nirodhaṃ dakkhanto paṭipannakoti vattabboti  
              
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  nirodhe diṭṭhe  phale ṭhitoti vattabboti  
  
 pa paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
                 
  
    sa pu  sotāpattiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo maggaṃ dakkhanto paṭipannākoti vattabbo  magge diṭṭhe phale ṭhitoti vattabboti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa anu  dukkhaṃ dakkhanto paṭipannakoti vattabbo  dukkhe diṭṭhe phale ṭhitoti vattabboti  
  
 pa paṭi na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  maggaṃ dakkhanto paṭipannakoti vattabbo  magge diṭṭhe phale ṭhitoti vattabboti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  samudayaṃ dakkhanto pe nirodhaṃ dakkhanto paṭipannakoti vattabbo  nirodhe diṭṭhe phale ṭhitoti vattabboti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  sotāpattiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo dukkhaṃ dakkhanto paṭipannakoti vattabbo  dukkhe diṭṭhe na vattabbaṃ phale ṭhitoti vattabboti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  maggaṃ dakkhanto paṭipannakoti vattabbo  magge diṭṭhe na vattabbaṃ phale ṭhitoti vattabboti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 sa pu  samudayaṃ dakkhanto pe nirodhaṃ dakkhanto paṭipannakoti vattabbo  nirodhe diṭṭhe na vattabbaṃ phale ṭhitoti vattabboti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  maggaṃ dakkhanto paṭipannakoti vattabbo  magge diṭṭhe na vattabbaṃ phale ṭhitoti vattatabboti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sotāpattiphalasacchikiriyāya paṭipanno puggalo dukkhaṃ dakkhanto paṭipannakoti vattabbo  dukkhe diṭṭhe na vattabbaṃ phale ṭhitoti vattabboti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
                 
  
 sa anu  niratthiyaṃ  dukkhadassananti  
              
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  samudayaṃ dakkhanto pe nirodhaṃ dakkhanto paṭipannakoti vattabbo  nirodhe diṭṭhe na vattabbaṃ phale ṭhitoti vattabboti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  niratthiyaṃ nirodhadassananti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    pa pu  dukkhe diṭṭhe cattāri saccāni diṭṭhāni hontīti  
 sa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 pa anu  dukkhasaccaṃ cattāri ariyasaccānīti  
  
 sa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  rūpakkhaṇdhe aniccato diṭṭhe pañcakkhaṇdhā aniccato diṭṭhā hontīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  rūpakkhaṇdho pañcakkhaṇdhoti  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  cakkhāyatane aniccato diṭṭhe dvādasāyatanāni aniccato diṭṭhāni honitīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa anu  cakkhāyatanaṃ dvādasāyatanānīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  cakkhudhātuyā aniccato diṭṭhāya aṭṭhārasadhātuyo aniccato diṭṭhā hontīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  cakkhudhātu aṭṭhārasa dhātuyoti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  cakkhuṇdiraye aniccato diṭṭhe bāvīsatiṇdirayāni aniccato diṭṭhāni hontīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  cakkhuṇdirayaṃ bāvīsatiṇdirayānīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    nidatthiyaṃ  sīmu  
  
                 
  
    sa pu  catūhi ñāṇehi sotipattiphalaṃ sacchikarotīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  cattāri sotāpattiphalānītī  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  aṭṭhahi ñāṇehi sotāpattiphalaṃ sacchikarotīti  
              
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  aṭṭha sotāpattiphalānīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  dvādasahi ñāṇehi sotāpattiphalaṃ sacchikarotīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  dvādasa sotāpattiphalānīti  
  
 pa pa ṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbai pe 
  
    sa pu  catucattārīsāya ñāṇehi sotāpattiphalaṃ sacchikarotīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  catucattārīsaṃ sotāpattiphalānīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  sattasattatiyā ñāṇehi sotāpattiphalaṃ sacchikarotīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  sattasattati sotāpattiphalānīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    pa pu  na vattabbaṃ anupubbābhisamayoti  
  
 sa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 pa anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā seyyathāpi bhikkhave mahāsamuddo anupubbaninno anupubbapoṇo anupbbapabbhāro na āyatakeneva papāto  evameva kho bhikkhave imasmiṃ dhammavinaye anupubbasikkhā anupubbakiriyā anupubbapaṭipadā na āyatakeneva aññāpaṭivedhoti a  attheva suttantoti  
  
 sa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 anu pā  tena hi anupubbābhisamayoti 
  
  a   aṭṭhakaṅguttara  mahāvagga  uposathasutta  
  
                 
  
    pa pu  na vattabbaṃ anupubbābhisamayoti  
  
 sa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 pa anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  
 anupubbena medhāvī 
 thokathokaṃ khaṇe khaṇe kammāro rajatasseva 
 niddhame malamattanoti a  
  
 attheva suttantoti  
  
 sa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 anu pā  tena hi anupubbābhisamayoti   
              
    sa pu  anupubbābhisamayoti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  naṇvāyasmā gavampatī thero bhikkhū etadavoca  sammukhā metaṃ āvuso bhagavato sutaṃ  sammukhā paṭiggahītaṃ  yo bhikkhave dukkhaṃ passati dukkhasamudayampi so passati dukkhanirodhampi passati dukkhanirodhagāminiṃ paṭipadampi passati  yo dukkhasamudayaṃ passati dukkhampi so passati dukkhanirodhampi passati dukkhanirodhagāminiṃ paṭipadampi passati  yo dukkhanirodhaṃ passati dukkhampi so passati dukkhasamudayampi passati dukkhanirodhagāminiṃ paṭipadampi passati  yo dukkhanirodhagāminiṃ paṭipadaṃ passati dukkhampi so passati dukkhasamudayampi passati dukkhanirodhampi passatīti b  attheva suttantoti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 anu pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ anupubbābhisamayoti  
  
    sa pu  anupubbābhisamayoti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
    tena hi vattabbaṃ anupubbābhisamayoti  sīmu  
  a   dhammapada  malavagga 
  b   saccasaṃyutta  koṭigāmavagga  gavampatisutta  
  
                 
  
 sa anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  
 sahāvassadassanasampadāya 
 tayassu dhammā jahitā bhavanti  
 sakkāyadiṭṭhivicikicchitañca 
 sīlabbataṃ vāpi yadatthi kiñci  
 catūhapāyehi ca vippamutto 
 cha cābhiṭhānāni abhabbo kātunti  a  
  
 attheva suttantoti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 anu pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ anupubbābhisamayoti  
  
    sa pu  anupubbābhisamayoti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā  yasmiṃ bhikkhave samaye ariyasāvakassa virajaṃ vītamalaṃ dhammacakkhuṃ udapādi  yaṃ kiñci samudayadhammaṃ sabbaṃ taṃ nirodhadhammanti  sahadassanuppādā bhikkhave ariyasāvakassa tīṇi saññojanāni pahīyanti  sakkāyadiṭṭhi vicikicchā sīlabbataparāmāsoti attheva suttantoti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 anu pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ anupubbābhisamayoti  
  
 anupubbābhisamayakathā              niṭṭhitā  
  
  
  a   suttanipāta  ratanasuttaṃ  
  
                 
  
 vohārakathā 
  
   sa pu  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaroti  
  
 pa paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 sa anu  lokuttare sote paṭihaññati no lokiyo  lokuttarena viññānena paṭivijānanti no lokiyena  sāvakā paṭivijānanti no puthujjanāti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
   sa pu  nanu buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokiye sote paṭihaññatīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā āmantā  
 anu ṭha  hañci buddhassa bhagavato vohāre lokiye sote paṭihaññati  
  
 anu pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokutataroti  
  
   sa pu  nanu buddhassa bhagavato vohāraṃ lokiyena viññāṇena paṭivijānantīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 anu ṭha  hañci buddhassa bhagavato vohāraṃ lokiyena viññāṇena paṭivijānanti  
  
 anu pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaroti  
  
   sa pu  nanu buddhassa bhagavato vohāraṃ puthujjanā paṭivijānantīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 anu ṭha  hañci buddhassa bhagavato vohāraṃ puthujjanā paṭivijānanti  
  
 anu pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaroti  
  
                 
  
   sa pu  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaroti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  magge phalaṃ nibbānaṃ sotāpattimaggo sotāpattiphalaṃ sakadāgāmimaggo sakadāgāmiphalaṃ anāgāmimaggo anāgāmiphalaṃ arahattamaggo arahattaphalaṃ satipaṭṭhānaṃ sammappadhānaṃ iddhipādo iṇdirayaṃ balaṃ bojjhaṅgoti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
   sa pu  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaroti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  atthi keci buddhassa bhagavato vohāraṃ suṇantīti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā               
  
 sa anu  lokuttaro dhammo sotaviññeyyo sotasmiṃ paṭihaññati  sotassa āpāthaṃ āgacchatīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
   sa pu  nanu lokuttaro dhamme na sotaviññeyyo na sotasmiṃ paṭihaññati  na sotassa āpāthā āgacchatīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 anu ṭha  hañci lokuttaro dhammo na sotaviññeyyo na sotasmiṃ paṭihaññati na sotassa āpāthaṃ āgacchati  
 anu pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaroti  
  
   sa pu  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaroti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  atthi keci buddhassa bhagavato vohāre rajjeyyunti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  lokuttaro dhammo rāgaṭṭhāniyo rajanīyo kamanīyo madanīyo baṇdhanīyo mucchanīyoti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
                 
  
   sa pu  nanu lokuttaro dhammo na rāgaṭṭhāniyo na rajanīyo na kamanīyo na madanīyo na baṇdhanīyo na mucchanīyoti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 anu ṭha  hañci lokuttaro dhammo na rāgaṭṭhāniyo na rajanīyo na kamanīyo na madanīyo na baṇdhanīyo na mucchanīyo  
  
 anu pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaroti  
  
    sa pu  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaroti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  atthi keci buddhassa bhagavato vohāre dusseyyunti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  lokuttaro dhammo dosaṭṭhānīyo kopaṭṭhānīyo paṭighaṭṭhānīyoti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  nanu lokuttaro dhamme na dosaṭṭhānīyo na kopaṭṭhānīyo na paṭighaṭṭhānīyoti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 anu ṭha  hañci lokuttaro dhammo na dosaṭṭhānīyo na kopaṭṭhānīyo              na paṭighaṭṭhānīyo  
  
 anu pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaroti  
  
    sa pu  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaroti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  atthi keci buddhassa bhagavato vohāre muyheyyunti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
                 
  
 sa anu  lokuttaro dhammo mohaṭṭhāniyo aññāṇakaraṇo acakkhukaraṇo paññānirodhiko vighātapakkhiko anibbānasaṃvattanikoti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  nanu lokuttaro dhammo na mohaṭṭhāniyo na aññāṇakaraṇo na acakkhukaraṇo paññāvuddhiko  avighātapakkhiko nibbānasaṃvattanikoti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 anu ṭha  hañci lokuttaro dhammo na mohaṭṭhāniyo na aññāṇakaraṇo na acakkhukaraṇo paññāvuddhiko  avighātapakkhiko nibbānasaṃvattaniko 
  
 anu pā  no ca vata re vattabbe  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaroti  
  
    sa pu  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokuttaroti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  ye keci buddhassa bhagavato vohāraṃ suṇanti  sabbe te maggaṃ bhāventīti  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  ye keci buddhassa bhagavato vohāraṃ suṇanti  sabbe te maggaṃ bhāventīti 
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  bālaputhujjanā buddhassa bhagavato vohāraṃ suṇanti  bālaputhujjanā maggaṃ bhāvettīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 sa anu  mātughātakā  pe pitughātakā pe arahantaghātakā peruhiruppādakā pe saṅghabhedakā buddhassa bhagavato vohāraṃ sūṇanti  saṅghabhedakā maggaṃ bhāventīti   
  
 pa paṭi  va hevaṃ vattabbe pe              
    paññāvuḍḍhiko  sīmu  
    mātughātako maggaṃ bhāveti  sīmu  machasaṃ  
    machasaṃ  sīmu potthakesu vākyamidaṃ ekatte ṭhapitaṃ dissate  
  
                 
  
    pa pu  labbhā sovaṇṇamayāya laṭṭhiyā dhaññapuñjopi suvaṇṇapuñjopi ācikkhitunti  
  
 sa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 anu pā  evamevaṃ bhagavā lokuttarena vohārena lokiyampi lokuttarampi dhammaṃ voharatīti  
  
    sa pu  labbhā eḷaṇḍiyāya laṭṭhiyā dhaññapuñjopi suvaṇṇapuñjāpi acikkhitunti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 anu pā  evamevaṃ bhagavā lokiyena vohārena lokiyampi lokuttarampi dhammaṃ voharatiti  
  
    sa pu  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokiyaṃ voharantassa lokiyā hoti  lokuttairaṃ voharantassa lokuttaro hotīti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  lokiyaṃ voharantassa lokiye sote paṭihaññati  lokuttaraṃ voharantassa lokuttare sote paṭihaññati  lokiyaṃ voharantassa lokiyena viññāṇena paṭivijānanti  lokuttaraṃ voharantassa lokuttarena viññāṇena paṭivijānanti  lokiyaṃ voharantassa puthujjanā paṭivijānanti  lokuttaraṃ voharantassa sāvakā paṭivijānantīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    pa pu  na vattabbaṃ buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokiyaṃ voharantassa lokiyo hoti  lokuttaraṃ voharantassa lokuttaro hotīti  
  
 sa paṭiññā āmantā  
 pa anu  nanu bhagavā lokiyampi lokuttarampi dhammaṃ voharatīti  
  
 sa paṭiññā āmantā  
  
                 
  
 anu ṭha  hañci bhagavā lokiyampi lokuttarampi dhammaṃ voharati  
  
 anu pā  tena vata re vattabbe  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokiyaṃ voharantassa lokiyo hoti  lokuttaraṃ voharantassa lokuttaro hotīti  
  
    sa pu  buddhassa bhagavato vohāro lokiyaṃ voharantassa lokiyo hoti  lokuttaraṃ voharantassa lokuttaro hotīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  maggaṃ voharantassa magge hoti  amaggaṃ voharantassa              amaggo hoti  phalaṃ voharantassa phalaṃ hoti  aphalaṃ voharantassa aphalaṃ hoti  nibbānaṃ voharantassa nibbānaṃ hoti  anibbānaṃ voharantassa anibbānaṃ hoti  saṅkhataṃ voharantassa saṅkhataṃ hoti  asaṅkhataṃ voharantassa asaṅkhataṃ hoti  rūpaṃ voharantassa rūpaṃ hoti  arūpaṃ voharantassa arūpaṃ hoti  vedanaṃ voharantassa vedanā hoti  avedanaṃ voharantassa avedanā hoti  saññaṃ voharantassa saññā hoti  asaññaṃ voharantassa asaññā hoti  saṅkhāre voharantassa saṅkhārā honti  asaṅkhāre voharantassa asaṅkhārā honti  viññāṇaṃ voharantassa viññāṇaṃ hoti  aviññāṇaṃ voharantassa aviññāṇaṃ hotīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 vohārakathā niṭṭhitā  
  
                 
  
 nirodhakathā 
  
   sa pu  dve nirodhāti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  dve dukkhanirodhāti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
   sa pu  dve dukkhanirodhāti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  dve nirodhasaccānīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
   sa pu  dve nirodhasaccānīti  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  dve dukkhasaccānīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
   sa pu  dve nirodhasaccānīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  dve samudayasaccānīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
   sa pu  dve nirodhasaccānīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā               
  
 sa anu  dve maggasaccānīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
                 
  
   sa pu  dve nirodhasaccānīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 sa anu  dve tāṇāni pe dve leṇāni pe dve saraṇāni pe dve parāyanāni pe dve accutāni pe dve amatāni pe dve nibbānānīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
   sa pu  dve nibbānānīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 sa anu  atthi dvinnaṃ nibbānānaṃ uccanīcatā  hīnappaṇītatā  ukkaṃsāvakaṃso  sīmā vā bhedo vā  rājī vā antarikā vāti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
   sa pu  dve nirodhāti  
  
 pa paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 sa anu  nanu appaṭisaṅkhāniruddhe saṅkhāre paṭisaṅkhā nirodhentīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 anu ṭha  hañci appaṭisaṅkhāniruddhe saṅkhāre paṭisaṅkhā nirodhenti  
 anu pā  no ca vata re vattabbe dve nirodhāti  
  
   pa pu  na vattabbaṃ dve nirodhāti  
  
 sa paṭiññā āmantā  
  
 pa anu  nanu appaṭisaṅkhāniruddhāpi saṅkhārā accantabhaggā  paṭisaṅkhāniruddhāpi saṅkhārā accantabhaggāti  
  
 sa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 anu ṭha  hañci appaṭisaṅkhāniruddhāpi saṅkhārā accantabhaggā  paṭisaṅkhāniruddhāpi saṅkhārā accantabhaggā  
  
 anu pā  tena vata re vattabbe dve nirodhāti  
  
                 
  
    sa pu  dve va nirodhāti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  paṭisaṅkhāniruddhāpi saṅkhārā ariyamaggaṃ āgamma niruddhāti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
              
 sa anu  appaṭisaṅkhāniruddhāpi saṅkhārā ariyamaggaṃ āgamma niruddhāti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa pu  dve nirodhāti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  paṭisaṅkhāniruddhā saṅkhārā na puna uppajjantīti  
  
 pa paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa anu  appaṭisaṅkhāniruddhā saṅkhārā na puna uppajjantīti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 anu pā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ  dve nirodhāti  
  
 nirodhakathā niṭṭhitā  
  
 dutiyo vaggo niṭṭhito  
  
 tassa uddānaṃ  
 parūpahāro aññāṇaṃ 
 kaṅkhā paravitaraṇā 
 vacībhedo dukkhāhāro 
 cittaṭṭhiti ca kukkuḷā 
 ekābhisamayo ceva 
 vohāro ca nirodhakoti

 dutiyo bhāgo 
 namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa 
 tatiyo vaggo 
       balakathā 
  
    sa  pu  tathāgatabalaṃ sāvakasādhāraṇanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 sa  anu  tathāgatabalaṃ sāvakapalaṃ  sāvakabalaṃ tathāgata balanti  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
    sapu  tathāgatabalaṃ sāvakasādhāraṇanti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  taññeva tathāgatabalaṃ taṃ sāvakabalaṃ  
 taññeva sāvakabalaṃ taṃ tathāgatabanti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
    sapu  tathāgatabalaṃ sāvakasādhāraṇanti

 yādisaṃ sāvakabalaṃ tādisaṃ tathāgatabalanti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
            
    sapu  tathāgatabalaṃ sāvakasādhāraṇanti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  yādiso tathāgatassa pubbayogo pubbacariyā  
 dhammakkhānaṃ dhammadesanā  tādiso sāvakassa pubbayogo pubbacariyā  dhammakkhānaṃ dhammadesanāti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
    sapu  tathāgatabalaṃ sāvakasādhāraṇanti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa anu  thāgato jino satthā sammāsambuddho sabbaññu sabbadassāvī dhammassāmi  dhammapaṭisaraṇoti  
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sāvako jino satthā sammāsambuddho sabbaññu sabbadassāvī dhammassāmi dhammapaṭisaraṇoti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
    sa  pu  tathāgatabalaṃ sāvakasādhāraṇanti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  tathāgato anuppannassa maggassa uppadetā  
 asañajātassa              maggassa sañajanetā  anakkhātassa maggassa akkhātā  
 maggaññu maggavidu maggakovidoti  
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sāvako anuppannassa maggassa uppādetā  
 asañjātassa maggassa sañjanetā  anakkhātassa maggassa akkhātā 
 maggaññu maggavidu maggakovidoti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
    sa  pu  indriyaparopariyattaṃ yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ sāvakasādhāraṇanti 
  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sāvako sabbaññu sabbadassāviti  
  
 pa paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
            
    pa  pu  sāvako ṭhānāṭhānaṃ jānātīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci sāvako ṭhānāṭhānaṃ jānāti  
 anu  pā  tena vata re vattabbe ṭhānāṭhānaṃ yathābhūtaṃ 
 ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ sāvakasādhāraṇanti  
  
    sāvako atītānāgatapaccappannānaṃ kammasamādānānaṃ ṭhānaso hetuso vipākaṃ jānātīti  
 sa  paṭiññā amāntā  anu  ṭha  hañci sāvako atītānāgatapaccuppannānaṃ kammasamādānānaṃ 
 ṭhānaso hetuso vipākaṃ jānāti  
  
 anu  pā tena vata re vattabbe  atītānāgatapaccuppannānaṃ kammasamādānānaṃ 
 ṭhānaso hetuso vipākaṃ yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ 
 sāvakasādhāraṇanti

      ariyannikathā  
    sa  pu  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyanti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  maggo phalaṃ nibbānaṃ sotāpattimaggo 
 sotāpattiphalaṃ sakadāgāmimaggo sakadāgāmiphalaṃ 
 anāgāmimaggo anāgāmiphalaṃ arahattamaggo 
 arahattaphalaṃ satipaṭṭhānaṃ sammappadhānaṃ iddhipādo 
 indriyaṃ balaṃ bojjhaṅgoti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyanti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  suññatārammaṇanti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  suññatārammaṇanti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  ṭhānāṭhānañca manasikaroti  suññatañca manasikarotiti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    ṭhānāṭhānañca manasikaroti  suññatañca manasikarotīti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  dvinnaṃ phassānaṃ dvinnaṃ cittānaṃ samodhānaṃ hotīti               
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyanti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  animittārammaṇaṃ  pe appaṇibhitārammaṇanti 
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
             
    sa  pu  appaṇihitārammaṇanti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  ṭhānaṭhānañca manasikaroti  appaṇihitañca manasikarotīti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe

 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  dvinnaṃ phassānaṃ dvinnaṃ cittānaṃ samodhānaṃ hotīti

    sa  pu  satipaṭṭhānā ariyā suññatārammaṇāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ suññatārammaṇānti  sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  satipaṭṭhānā ariyā suññatārammaṇā peappaṇihitārammaṇāti               
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ appahitārammaṇānti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  sammappadhānā iddhipādā  indriyābalābojjhaṅgā 
 ariyā suññatārammaṇāti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ suññatārammaṇānti  sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
             
     sa  pu  bojjhaṅgā ariyā animittārammaṇā pe 
 appaṇihitārammaṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ 
 appaṇihitārammaṇanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabba pe 
  
     sa  pu  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ 
 ariyaṃ na vattabbaṃ suññatārammaṇanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  satipaṭṭhānā ariyā  na vattabbā suññatārammaṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ 
 ariyaṃ na vattabbaṃ animittārammaṇanti  peappaṇihitārammaṇanta 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  satipaṭṭhānā ariyā  na vattabbā appaṇihitārammaṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ 
 ariyaṃ na vattabbaṃ suññatārammaṇaṇaṃ pe animittārammaṇaṃ peappaṇihitārammaṇanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sammappadhānaṃ pe bojjhaṅgā ariyā  na vattabbā appaṇihitārammaṇāti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  sattānaṃ cutupapāte yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyanti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  maggo phalaṃ nibbānaṃ sotāpattamaggo 
 sotāpattiphalaṃ pe bojjhaṅgoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
             
     sa  pu  sattānaṃ cutupapāte yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyanti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  suññatārammaṇanti 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
              
     sa  pu  suññatārammaṇanti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sattānaṃ cutupapānañca manasikaroti  suññatañca manasikarotīti  pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  sattānaṃ cutupapātañca manasikaroti  suññatañca manasikarotīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  dvinnaṃ phassānaṃ dvinnaṃ cittānaṃ samodhānaṃ hotīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  sattānaṃ cutupapāte yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyanti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  animittārammaṇaṃ pe appaṇihārammaṇanti 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  appaṇihitārammaṇanti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sattānaṃ cutupapātañca manasikaroti  appaṇibhitañca manasikarotīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  sattānaṃ cutupapātañca manasikaroti  appaṇihitañca manasikarotīti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  dvinnaṃ phassānaṃ dvinnaṃ cittānaṃ samodhānaṃ hotīti  pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
             
     sa  pu satipaṭṭhānā ariyā  suññatārammaṇā pe 
 animittārammaṇā pe appaṇihitārammaṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sattānaṃ cutupapāte yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ 
 tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ appaṇihitārammaṇanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
              
     sa  pu  sammappadhānaṃ pe bojjhaṅgā ariyā 
 suññatārammaṇā pe animittārammaṇā pe 
 appaṇihitārammaṇāti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sattānaṃ cutupapāte yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ 
 ariyaṃ  appaṇihitārammaṇanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  sattānaṃ cutupapāte yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgabalaṃ ariyaṃ  
 na vattabbaṃ suññatārammaṇaṃ peanimittārammaṇaṃ pe 
 appaṇihitārammaṇanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  satipaṭṭhānā ariyā  vattabbā appaṇihitārammaṇati  pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  sattānaṃ cutupapāte yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ 
 na vattabbaṃ suññatārammaṇaṃ peanimittārammaṇaṃ 
 pe appaṇihitārammaṇanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sammappadhānā pe bojjhaṅgā ariyā  na vattabbārammaṇa pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
             
     pa  su  asavānaṃ khaye yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyanti 
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyanti 
 sapaṭi  na heva ṃvattabbe pe 
              
     pa  su  asavānaṃ khaye yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyanti 
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  sattānaṃ cutupapāte yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyanti 
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     pa  su  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ na vattabbaṃ ariyanti 
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  āsavānaṃ khaye yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyanti 
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     pa  su  sattānaṃ cutupapāte yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ vattabbaṃ ariyanti 
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  āsavānaṃ khaye yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ na vattabbaṃ ariyanti 
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     pa  su  asavānaṃ khaye yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ suññatārammaṇanti 
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ suññatārammaṇanti 
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     pa  su  asavānaṃ khaye yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ 
 animittārammaṇaṃ pe appaṇihitārammaṇanti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
             
 pa  anu  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ  
 appaṇihitārammaṇanti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     pa  su  asavānaṃ khaye yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ 
 suññatārammaṇaṃ pe animittārammaṇaṃ peappaṇihitārammaṇanti 
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  sattānaṃ cutuppāte yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ 
 appaṇihitārammaṇanti 
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
              
     pa  su  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ 
 na vattabbā suññatārammaṇanti 
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  āsavānaṃ khaye yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ 
 na vattabbaṃ suññatārammaṇanti 
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     pa  su  ṭhānāṭhāne yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ 
 na vattabbaṃ animittārammaṇaṃ peappaṇihitārammaṇanti 
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  āsavānaṃ khaye yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ 
 na vattabbaṃ appaṇihitārammaṇanti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     pa  su  sattānaṃ cutupapāte yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ 
 na vattabbaṃ suññatārammaṇaṃ peanimittārammaṇā pe 
 appaṇihitārammaṇanti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  āsāvānaṃ khaye yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇaṃ tathāgatabalaṃ ariyaṃ 
 na vattabbaṃ appaṇihitārammaṇanti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
 ariyayatikathā niṭṭhitā  
  
             
      vimuttikathā  
    sa  pu  sarāgaṃ cittaṃ vimuccatīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 rāgasahagataṃ rāgasahajātaṃ rāgasaṃsaṭṭhaṃ 
 rāgasampayuttaṃ rāgasahabhu rāgānuparivatti 
 akusalaṃ lokiyaṃ sāsavaṃ saṃyojaniyaṃ ganthanīyaṃ 
 oghanīyaṃ  yoganīyaṃ  nīvaraṇiyaṃ parāmaṭṭhaṃ 
 upādāniyaṃ saṃkilesikaṃ  cittaṃ vimuccatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  saphassaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  phasso ca cittaṃ ca ubho vimuccantiti pa  paṭiññā  āmantā               
 sa  anu  sarāgaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  rago ca cittaṃ ca ubho vimuccantīti  
  
    sa  pu  savedanaṃ pe sasaññaṃ pe sacetanaṃ 
 pe sasaññaṃ  cittaṃ vimuccati  saññā ca cittaṃ 
 ca ubho vimuccantīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sarāgaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  rāgo ca cittaṃ ubho vimuccati  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  saphassaṃ sarāgaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  phasso ca cittā ca ubho 
 vimuccantīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  rāgo ca cittaṃ ca ubho vimuccantīti 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    oghaniyaṃ  sīmu  machasaṃ  syā    yoganiyaṃ  sīmu  machasaṃ  syā    saṃkilesiyaṃ  sīmu  machasaṃ    sapaññaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
             
    sa  pu  savedanaṃ sarāgaṃ pe sasaññaṃ sarāgaṃ pe 
 sacetanaṃ sarāgaṃ pe sasaññaṃ sarāgaṃ 
 cittaṃ vimuccati  saññā ca cittaṃ ca uho vimuccantiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  rāgo ca cittañca ubho vimuccantiti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  sadosaṃ cittaṃ vimuccatiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 dosahagataṃ dosasahajātaṃ dosasaṃsaṭṭhaṃ 
 dosasampayuttaṃ dosasahabhu dosānuparivatti 
 akusalaṃ lokiyaṃ sāsavaṃ saṃyojaniyaṃ ganthanīyaṃ 
 oghanīyaṃ yoganīyaṃ nīvaraṇiyaṃ parāmaṭṭhaṃ 
 upādāniyaṃ saṃkilesikaṃ cittaṃ vimuccatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  saphassaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  phasso ca cittaṃ ca ubho vimuccantiti pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sadosaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  doso ca cittaṃ ca ubho vimuccantīti  
  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  savedanaṃ pe sasaññaṃ pe sacetanaṃ 
 pe sasaññaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  saññā ca cittaṃ 
 ca ubho vimuccantīti               
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sadosaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  doso ca cittaṃ ubho vimuccati  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  saphassaṃ dosaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  phasso ca cittā ca ubho 
 vimuccantīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sadosā cittaṃ vimuccati  doso ca cittaṃ ca ubho vimuccantīti 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
             
     sa  pu  savedanaṃ sadosaṃ pe sasaññaṃ sadosaṃ pesacetanaṃ sadosaṃ pe sasaññaṃ 
 sasaññaṃ sadosaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  saññā ca cittaṃ ca 
 ubho vimuccantīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  doso ca cittaṃ ca ubho vimuccantīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu samohaṃ cittaṃ vimuccatīti  pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
 mohasahagataṃ mohasahajātaṃ mohasaṃsaṭṭhaṃ 
 mohasampayuttaṃ mohasahabhu mohānuparivatti 
 akusalaṃ lokiyaṃ sāsavaṃ saṃyojaniyaṃ ganthanīyaṃ 
 oghanīyaṃ yoganīyaṃ nīvaraṇiyaṃ  parāmaṭṭhaṃ 
 upādāniyaṃ saṃkilesikaṃ  cittaṃ vimuccatīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  saphassaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  phasso ca cittaṃ ca ubho vimuccantiti pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sarāgaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  rago ca cittaṃ ca ubho vimuccantīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  savedanaṃ pe sasaññaṃ pe sacetanaṃ 
 pe sasaññaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  saññā ca cittaṃ 
 ca ubho vimuccantīti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  sarāgaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  moho ca cittaṃ ubho vimuccananti 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  saphassaṃ samohaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  phasso ca cittā ca ubho 
 vimuccantīti               
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  moho ca cittaṃ ca ubho vimuccantīti 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    saṃyojaniyaṃ        nīvaraṇiyaṃ        saṃkilesiyaṃ  sīmu  machasaṃ 
  
             
     sa  pu  savedanaṃ samohaṃ pe sasaññaṃ samohaṃ 
 pe sacetanaṃ samohaṃ pe sasaññaṃ 
 samohaṃ cittaṃ vimuccati  saññā ca cittaṃ ca 
 ubho vimuccantiti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  moho ca cittaṃ ca ubho vimuccantīti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ  sarāgaṃ sadosaṃ samohaṃ cittaṃ 
 vivuccatīti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 pa  anu  citarāgaṃ vitadosaṃ vitamohaṃ nikkilesaṃ 
 cittaṃ vimuccatīti  
 sa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 anu  ā  tena hi na vattabbā  sarāgaṃ sadosaṃ samohaṃ 
 cittaṃ vimuccatīti  
  
 vimuttikathā niṭṭhitā 
  
    ka vattabbanti  machasaṃ potthake natthi paramidampi natthi sakavādipucchā viya nidasikaṃ     ta vattabbanti      syāmapetthakesu na dissate 
  
             
      vimuccamānakathā 
    sa  pu  vimuttaṃ vimuccamānanti 
 pa  paṭaṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  ekadesaṃ vimutataṃ ekadesaṃ avimuttanti 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  ekadesaṃ vimuttaṃ  ekadesaṃ avimuttanti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  ekadesaṃ sotāpanno  ekadesā na 
 sotāpanno  ekadesaṃ sotāpattiphalappatto 
 paṭiladdho adhigato sacchikato 
 upasampajja viharati  kāyena phusitvā viharati  
 ekadesaṃ na kāyena phusitvā viharati  ekadesaṃ 
 sattakkhattuparamo kolaṃkolo ekabīji  
 buddhe aveccappasādena samannāgato  dhamme 
 pe saṅghe pe ariyakantehi sīlehi 
 na samannāgatoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  ekadesaṃ vimuttaṃ  ekadesaṃ avimuttanti 
              pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
  
 sa  anu  ekadesaṃ sakadāgāmī  ekadesaṃ na sakadāgāmī  
 ekadesaṃ sakadāgāmiphalappatto  paṭiladdho 
 adhigato sacchikato upasampajja viharati  
 kāyena phusītvā viharati  ekadesaṃ na kāyena 
 phusitvā viharatīti  
  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
             
    sa  pu  ekadesaṃ vimuttaṃ  ekadesaṃ avimuttanti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
  
 sa  anu  ekadesaṃ anāgāmi  ekadesaṃ na anāgāmi  
 ekadesaṃ anāgāmiphalappatto  paṭiladdho 
 adhigato sacchikato upasampajja viharati  
 kāyena phusītvā viharati  ekadesaṃ na kāyena 
 phusitvā viharatīti ekadesaṃ antarāparinibbāyī  
 upahacca parinibbāyī  asaṅkhāraparinibbāyī  
 sasaṅkhāraparinibbāyī  uddhaṃsoto akaṇiṭṭhagāmi  
 ekadesaṃ na uddhaṃsoto akaṇiṭṭhagāmīni  
  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  ekadesaṃ vimuttaṃ  ekadesaṃ avimuttanti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
  
 sa  anu  ekadesaṃ arahā  ekadesaṃ na arahā  ekadesaṃ 
 arahattappatto  paṭiladdho adhigato sacchikato 
 upasampajja viharati  kāyena phusītvā   viharati  ekadesaṃ vitarāgo vitadoso vitamoho 
 pe ekadosaṃ sacchikātabbā sacchikataṃ  
 ekadesaṃ saccikātabbaṃ na saccikatanti  
  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  vimuttaṃ vimuccamānanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  uppādakkhaṇe vimuttaṃ  bhavaṅgakkhaṇe vimuttanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabe pe 
  
    pa  pu  na vattabbaṃ vimuttaṃ vimuccamānanti  
 sa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
  
    kāyena na phusitvā     
  
             
 pa  anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā tassa evaṃ jānato evaṃ 
 passato kāmāsavāpi cittaṃ vimuccati  bhavāsavāpi 
 cittaṃ vimuccati  avijjāsavāpi cittaṃ 
 vimuccatiti a  attheva suttantoti               
 sa  paṭi  āmantā  
 anu  ā  tena hi vimuttaṃ vimuccamānanti  
  
    sa  pu  vimuttaṃ vimuccamānanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā  
 sa  anu  nanu vuttaṃ bhagavatā so evaṃ samāhite 
 citte parisuddhe pariyodāte anaṅgaṇe 
 vigatupakkilese mudubhute kammaniye ṭhite 
 āneñajappatte āsavānaṃ khayañāṇāya cittaṃ 
 abhininnāmetiti a  attheva suttantoti  
  
 sa  paṭi  āmantā  
 anu  ā  tena hi na vattabbaṃ vimuttaṃ vimuccamānanti  
  
    sa  pu  atthi cittaṃ vimuccamānanti  
 sa  paṭi  āmantā  
 sa  anu  atthi cittaṃ rajjamānaṃ dussamānaṃ vuyhamānaṃ 
 kilissamānanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
 sa  anu  nanu rattañceva arattañca duṭṭhañceva 
 aduṭṭhañca muḷhañce amuḷhañca dhinnañceva 
 acchinnañca bhinnañce abhinnañca katañceva 
 akatañcāti  
 sa  paṭi  āmantā  
 anu  ṭha  hañci rattañceva arattañca duṭṭhañceva 
 aduṭṭhañca muḷhañce amuḷhañca chinnañceva 
 acchinnañca bhinnañceva abhinnañca katañceva 
 akatañca  
 anu  pā  no ca vata re vattabbe atthi cittaṃ 
 vimuccamānanti  
  
 vimuccamānakathā niṭṭhitā  
  
    dighanikāya  sāmaññaphalasuttādisu  
  
             
      aṭṭhamakakathā 
    sa  pu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa diṭṭhipariyuṭṭhānaṃ pahīnanti  
 pa  paṭiññā āmantā 
 sa  anu  aṭṭhamako puggalo sotāpanno  sotāpattiphalappatto 
 paṭiladdho adhigato sacchikato 
 upasampajja viharati  kāyena phusitvā viharatīti 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa vicikicchāpariyuṭṭhānaṃ pahīnanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
              sa  anu  aṭṭhamako puggalo sotāpanno  sotāpattiphalappatto 
 pe kāyena phusitvā viharatīti 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa diṭṭhipariyuṭṭhānaṃ pahīnanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  aṭṭhamako puggalassa diṭṭhānusayo  pahīnoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa diṭṭhipariyuṭṭhānaṃ pahīnanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa vicikicchānusayo sīlabbataparāmāso pahīnoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
             
    sa  pu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa vicikicchāpariyuṭṭhānaṃ pahīnanti  pa  paññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa vivikicchānusayopahīnoti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa vicikicchāpariyuṭṭhānaṃ pahinanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa diṭṭhānusaso silabbataparāmāso pahīnoti pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa diṭṭhānusase appahīnoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa diṭṭhipariyuṭṭhānaṃ appahinanti 
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa diṭṭhānusaso appahīnoti 
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa vicikicchāpariyuṭṭhānaṃ appahīnanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
    sa  pu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa vicikicchānusayo 
 silabbataparāmāso appahīnoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
              sa  anu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa diṭṭhipariyuṭṭhānaṃ appahinanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa sīlabbataparāmāso appahīnoti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa vicikicchāpariyuṭṭhānaṃ appahīnanti  
 pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
             
     sa  pu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa diṭṭhipariyuṭṭhānaṃ pahīnanti  pa  paññā  āmantā 
 sa  anu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa diṭṭhipariyuṭṭhānappahānāya 
 maggo bhāvitoti  pa  paṭi  na hevaṃ vattabbe pe 
  
     sa  pu  aṭṭhamakassa puggalassa diṭṭhipariyuṭṭhānaṃ pahinanti  
 pa  paṭiññā  āmantā
